<form><strong style="color:darkred; font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size:14pt">瑜伽師地論科句披尋記卷第六十二</strong></form>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:#000000"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　彌勒菩薩說</span></span></span><br />
<a name="62p4965"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:#000000"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　唐三藏沙門玄奘奉詔譯</span></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:#000000"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　韓清淨科記</span></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">攝決擇分中三摩呬多地之一</span></strong></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丙三、三摩呬多地3　丁一、結前生後</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科三摩呬多地，主要是說禪定，從未到地定，一直到四空定，乃至滅盡定，包括世間及出世間的禪定，分三科；第一科結前生後，結束前文，生起後文。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是已說有尋有伺等三地決擇。三摩呬多地決擇，我今當說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　從卷58到卷61已經說過〈有尋有伺〉等三地決擇。現在是〈三摩呬多地〉的決擇，也稱為等引地，主要決擇與禪定有關的諸法，我（彌勒菩薩）現在應該要說一說這件事。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丁二、隨應決擇3　戊一、總辨等引7　己一、辨彼障2　庚一、略標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨應決擇，隨順解釋應該決擇的諸法，分三科；第一科總辨等引，總相辨明與禪定有關的諸法，又分七科；第一科辨彼障，說明得世間及出世間禪定的障礙，又分二科；第一科略標，要略的標示出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="60734:49460"></a><a name="53391:49460"></a><a name="30327:49460"></a>謂補特伽羅，多隨煩惱染汙相續，不能正證心一境性。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若是有情，有很多的隨煩惱染汙身心，就會障礙修習禪定，不能與正見相應而證得世間及出世間的心一境性。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是隨煩惱，窺基大師說：隨煩惱是指：隨惱於心名隨煩惱；又心也隨煩惱而生，名隨煩惱。〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷58詳細說明：無慚、無愧等隨煩惱由四相差別建立：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、通一切不善心起，包括無慚、無愧；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、通一切染汙心起，通一切處三界所繫，包括放逸、掉舉、惛沈、不信、懈怠、邪欲、邪勝解、邪念、散亂、不正知等十種隨煩惱；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、於各別不善心起，包括忿、恨、覆、惱、嫉、慳、誑、諂、憍、害十種隨煩惱，都是各別不善心起，若隨一生時必無第二；這十種都是欲界繫，除誑、諂、憍，因為誑及諂至初靜慮，憍通三界，誑諂憍若在上地唯無記性；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、通善不善無記心起，非一切處，非一切時，包括尋、伺、惡作、睡眠四種隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又說到諸隨煩惱，若在欲界，略於十二處轉。若能參考這段文配合此處所說，更能了解其中的道理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">庚二、別釋2　辛一、多隨煩惱3　壬一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別釋，各別解釋禪定的障礙，分二科；第一科多隨煩惱，解釋多隨煩惱的種類，又分三科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名為多隨煩惱？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱為多隨煩惱？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列舉出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p4966"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂有諂、誑、矯、詐、無慚無愧、不信、懈怠、忘念、不定、惡慧、慢緩、猥雜、趣向前行、捨遠離軛、於所學處不甚恭敬、不顧沙門、唯希活命不為涅槃而求出家。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　多隨煩惱包括諂、誑、矯、詐、無慚無愧、不信、懈怠、忘念、不定、惡慧、慢緩、猥雜、趣向前行、捨遠離軛、於所學處不甚恭敬、不顧沙門、唯希活命不為涅槃而求出家，若有以上諸多隨煩惱染汙身心，就會障礙修習禪定，不能正確的證得心一境性。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以下這段文請參見：《雜阿含經》卷18〈497經〉（大正2，130b9～13）：「若彼比丘諂曲、幻偽、欺誑、不信、無慚、無愧、懈怠、失念、不定、惡慧、慢緩、違於遠離、不敬戒律、不顧沙門、不勤修學、不自省察、為命出家、不求涅槃，如是等人，聞我舉罪則生瞋恚。」文中說到出家人若有諂曲等隨煩惱，若犯戒時，有人舉罪則生瞋恚，如是不能懺悔清淨，戒不清淨難以得定，由此可知隨煩惱能障礙行者證得禪定。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又《瑜伽論記》卷17會景說：就此十八隨煩惱中，或就根本（煩惱）或於根本煩惱上隨義假立，或別有體俱稟貪氣分而生。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處列出十八種隨煩惱，因無慚無愧合在一起說，因此依科解釋只有十七種，事實上總數有十八種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬三、釋2　癸一、別辨相17　子一、有諂</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科別辨相，各別說明各種隨煩惱的相狀，又分十七科；第一科有諂，說明有諂的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何有諂？謂自有過，而不能於大師、智者同梵行所，如實發露。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是有諂？行者不能得定的第一種原因，是因為有諂媚的隨煩惱，即諂曲不直的心，自己有過失時，不能在佛面前，或者是有智慧的人，包括菩薩、得聖道的聖人及同修離欲梵行的行者前，如其真實犯戒的相貌來發露所犯，有這樣的過失，不能得定。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈決擇‧聲聞地〉卷68說到，欲界中諂有八種行及七種事。云何八行？一、迷惑諂行，二、覆藏諂行，三、顯示諂行，四、結構諂行，五、恭順諂行，六、謀計諂行，七、推注諂行，八、現悲諂行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其中說到有覆藏諂行，這就是諂與覆的隨煩惱不同之處，諂的範圍較廣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、有誑</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科有誑，說明有欺誑的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何有誑？謂不真實顯己功德。彼實無德，而欲令他諸有智者同梵行等了知有德。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是有誑？行者不能得定的第二種原因，是因為有欺誑的隨煩惱。不是真實有功德，卻顯示自己有功德。這種人實際上沒有道德、沒有功德，可是卻於其他有智慧的聖人，或者修離欲梵行的行者前，表現出有功德的相狀，讓人誤以為他是很有道德的。如果有這種欺誑性，也不能得定。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、有矯2　丑一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科有矯，說明有矯詐的相狀，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何有矯？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是矯？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、釋2　寅一、舉毀犯</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科舉毁犯，舉例說明毁犯淨戒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂於增上戒毀犯尸羅，或於軌範毀犯軌範。由見聞疑，他所舉時，遂用餘事假託餘事，或設外言而相誘引，如經廣說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者不能得定的第三種原因，是因為有矯詐的隨煩惱。於增上戒中的根本戒有所毀犯，或於佛所制的包括入聚落，或者是搭衣持缽，行住坐臥四威儀等軌則規範也有毀犯。由於他人見到、聽到、或者是懷疑，而來舉發的時候，就用顧左右而言他的方法，來逃避犯戒的這件事情，或者是安立假設其他的語言轉移話題，引導他人不要再說他的過失，如經中所廣說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這段文主要說明行者依矯、詐等而有邪命，可參考〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷22，801頁所說：「彼由如是或依矯、詐，或邪妄語，或假現相，或苦研逼，或利求利種種狀相，而從他所非法希求所有衣服、飲食、臥具、病緣醫藥、諸資生具。非以正法而有所求，由非法故，說名邪命。」此外〈攝事分〉卷100，2923頁說：復有苾芻，利養恭敬欲愛現行，見有他人多饒財寶，眾所知識，具大福祐，則便親附殷重承事，非愛非敬，亦非樂法，專為利養恭敬因緣。如是思惟：攝取質直、忍辱、柔和，為依止師，我於其處隨意自在。彼於我所多有施為，而我於彼都無所作。如是思惟：攝取捷慧、愛樂修福同梵行者以為助伴，所有僧事及其餘事皆令彼作，我獨蕭然自得而住。如是或有毀犯禁戒，同梵行者正詰問時，便不分明、假託餘事而有所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、出增上</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科出增上，指出由諂、誑增上力故毁犯淨戒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p4967"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂由諂、誑增上力故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於增上戒毀犯尸羅，主要是由諂媚及欺誑這二種隨煩惱的力量使令自己產生這種「矯」的行為，而生起邪命法。由於有諂媚，就不能如實發露自己的過失，而且假託其他的語言，使他人不知道自己犯過，以免失去利養。因為有誑，雖然自己沒有功德，但是在他人面前顯示自己很有功德，由此獲得利養。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如經廣說者：謂依矯詐起邪命法故。如聲聞地已說其相。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/22.htm#49477:18879">陵本二十二卷九頁1918</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依矯偽、諂詐等不正當的方法獲得衣、食、財等邪命法，如〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷22，800頁所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子四、有詐</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科有詐，說明有詐的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何有詐？謂怖他故，或復於彼有所希故，雖有犯重而不發露，亦不現行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是有詐？行者不能得定的第四種原因，是因為有詐欺的隨煩惱。由於怖畏他人知道自己所犯的罪過，或者對他人有所希求，希望從他人那裡得到恭敬利養，雖然犯了重罪，並沒有發露出來，也不會表現出有重大的惡業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》亦不現行者：謂由怖他為因緣故，或復於彼有所希故，亦不現行重惡業故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於害怕他人知道，或者是對他人有所希求，因此不會現行重大的惡業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">非實意樂，詐於有智同梵行所，現行親愛、恭敬、軟善身語二業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　沒有真實的意樂，對於有智慧的同修梵行的行者處，以欺騙方式，假裝表現出很親愛、很恭敬、很柔軟的身及語二種業。如〈攝事分〉卷100所說：復有苾芻，恭敬、利養、欲愛現行。見有他人，多饒財寶，眾所知識，具大福祐，則便親附、殷重承事；非愛、非敬、亦非樂法，專為利養、恭敬因緣。如是思惟：攝取質直、忍辱、柔和為依止師，我於其處隨意自在。彼於我所多有施為；而我於彼都無所作。如是思惟：攝取捷慧、愛樂修福、同梵行者以為助伴；所有僧事及其餘事，皆令彼作，我獨蕭然自得而住‧‧‧等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》非實意樂等者：攝事分說：復有苾芻，恭敬利養欲愛現行，見有他人多饒財寶，眾所知識，具大福祐，則便親附殷重承事，非愛非敬，亦非樂法，專為利養恭敬因緣。乃至廣說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/100.htm#49482:75974">陵本一百卷七頁7490</a>）其義應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈攝事分〉說：又有比丘，喜歡恭敬利養，有愛欲的煩惱現行，看到其他擁有很多財富寶物，大家都認識的、福報很大的同梵行所，就去親近依附他，殷重懇切的奉承他、為他做事，然而內心並不是真實愛護敬重他，也不是真的喜歡聽聞佛法，只是為了可以得到很多利養恭敬的因緣而親近這樣的大德。乃至廣說有很多的不正思惟等，如〈攝事分〉卷100，2923頁所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子五、無慚無愧</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科無慚無愧，說明無慚無愧的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p4968"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何無慚無愧？謂觀於自、或復觀他，無所羞恥。故思毀犯，犯已不能如法出離，好為種種鬥訟違諍。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是無慚無愧？這是二種隨煩惱合在一起解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者不能得定的第五種及第六種原因，是因為有無慚無愧的隨煩惱。觀待於自己無慚，或者觀待於他人無愧，沒有羞恥心，故意想要犯戒，犯了，又不能如佛所說的法來出離犯戒的過失，歡喜與他人鬥爭、訴訟、違逆、諍論。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子六、不信</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科不信，說明不信的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何不信？謂於佛法僧心不清淨，於苦集滅道生不順解。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是不信？行者不能得定的第七種原因，是因為有不信三寶四諦的隨煩惱。對於佛法僧三寶內心不清淨，不是真實的恭敬佛、恭敬法、恭敬僧，對於苦集滅道四諦，不隨順佛所說的真理去了解。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子七、懈怠</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科懈怠，說明懈怠的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何懈怠？謂執睡眠、偃臥為樂，晝夜唐捐，捨眾善品。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是懈怠？行者不能得定的第八種原因，是因為有懈怠的隨煩惱。執著睡眠、躺臥為快樂，白白的浪費白天及晚上的時間，棄捨止觀等善品的修習。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子八、忘念</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科忘念，說明忘念的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何忘念？謂於久遠所作、所說，不能隨念，不令隨憶，不守根門，不正知住。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是忘念？行者不能得定的第九種原因，是因為有忘失正念的隨煩惱。對於過去很久以前所作的事情，所說的話，不能隨順憶念，也不令自己生起憶念，不守護六根，眼耳鼻舌身意六根任意的攀緣色聲香味觸法，不能正知而住，不能隨時正確的知道自己有沒有生起煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子九、不定</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科不定，說明不定的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何不定？謂於定地，下至作意亦不能得。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是不定？是指行者不能得定的第十種原因，是因為有不定的隨煩惱。於禪定的境界，乃至最初的未到地定都不能得到。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p4969"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》下至作意亦不能得者：謂未獲得色界定地所攝少分微妙正作意故。本地分中聲聞地說：由奢摩他所攝持故，心於所緣寂靜行轉。從是以後，於瑜伽行初修業者名有作意，始得墮在有作意數。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/32.htm#49495:26805">陵本三十二卷二十頁2665</a>）與彼相違，名不能得。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　下至作意也不能得，是指不能獲得色界禪定所攝的少分、微妙、正確的如理作意。〈本地分‧聲聞地〉說：由於修止所攝持故，心在所緣境上很寂靜的數數憶念，沒有昏沈掉舉等，稱為寂靜行轉。於等持以後，心裡能夠寂靜住，對於初修三乘觀行業處的人，稱為有作意，才能屬於有作意這一類，即證得未到地定。與這樣的境界相違，名為不能得。如〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷32，1060頁所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子十、惡慧</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十科惡慧，說明惡慧的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何惡慧？謂住自見取，執不平等，難捨言論。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是惡慧？行者不能得定的第十一種原因，是因為有惡慧的隨煩惱。安住在自己的不正見，取著自己的思想見解認為是正確的是最殊勝的，執著大自在天為一切法生起的因等各種不平等因論，並且很難棄捨這類不正言論。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》執不平等難捨言論者：謂如沙門、或婆羅門，起如是見，立如是論：凡諸世間所有士夫補特伽羅所受，彼一切或以自在變化為因，或餘丈夫變化為因。由彼起邪決定，謂此為諦為實，餘皆癡妄，是名執不平等。不了言說自性唯假，難可捨離，是名難捨言論。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如有一類外道出家人，或者是有學問的婆羅門，生起這樣的見解，安立這樣的言論：凡是世間所有的人，他們所受的一切境界，都是由大自在天變化而產生的，或者是其他的大梵天王為因生起的。由於這類外道出家人，或者是有學問的婆羅門，對於這樣的見解生起很決定的認同，於此不平等因論，認為是真理，認為是事實，其他的道理都是愚癡、迷妄，這樣名為執不平等。不能了解言說的自體唯是假想安立，言說的境界不是真實的，沒有辦法捨離這些言論，名為難捨言論。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子十一、慢緩</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十一科慢緩，說明慢緩的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何慢緩？謂不捷利，亦不明了。不自超舉，無所能為，不能以身供侍有智同梵行者。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是慢緩？行者不能得定的第十二種原因，是因為有慢緩的隨煩惱。心很遲鈍、不敏捷銳利，對於三寶四諦、修習止觀，沒有清淨的信心，也不清楚明了。不能超越、不能舉心精勤提升自己的戒定慧等，不能很勤力的供養、奉事有智慧的同梵行者。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂不捷利等者：所作愚鈍，名不捷利。心無淨信，名不明了。懈怠相應，名不超舉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所作之事愚癡遲鈍，名為不捷利。心中對三寶四諦、所要修的止觀，缺乏正確的認識，也沒有清淨的信心，名為不明了。對於修行的事，懈怠相應，不能進步或超越，名為不超舉。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子十二、猥雜2　丑一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十二科猥雜，說明猥雜的相狀，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p4970"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何猥雜？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是猥雜？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、釋2　寅一、樂雜住</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋猥雜有二種，一是內心的混雜，一是外表的、身相的混雜，分二科；第一科樂雜住，先說身相的混雜。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂樂與在家及出家眾共相雜住。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者不能得定的第十三種原因，是因為有猥雜的隨煩惱。猥就是卑鄙、或者是下賤，猥雜也可以稱為混雜。猥雜，是指行者喜歡與在家及出家眾共相雜住，由此於過去未來的貨財、親友，追念、思慕、憂慼纏心；於隨所聞所究竟法，不能如理作意思惟；見在家及出家眾歡娛雜處，或見惡友共相雜住，便生隨喜心樂趣入；同其喜同其憂；由此不能遠離寂靜，閑居修習止觀，應當知道這一切都是魔事。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、樂尋思</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科樂尋思，說明好樂尋思內心的混雜。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又樂尋思諸惡不善欲尋思等，乃至家勢相應尋思，多隨尋思、多隨伺察。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又好樂尋思種種惡不善的欲、恚、害、乃至家勢相應等八種尋思，常常隨順尋思、數數詳細伺察這些尋思，這是一種內心的猥雜。八種尋思於〈攝事分〉卷89有詳細說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子十三、趣向前行2　丑一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十三科趣向前行，說明趣向前行的相狀，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="20918:49510"></a>云何趣向前行？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是趣向前行？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、釋2　寅一、趣向</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科趣向，受用袈裟或衣服等所有利養的事。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂受僧祇、或復別人諸衣服等所有利養，或請僧祇及與別人，皆名趣向。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者不能得定的第十四種原因，是因為有趣向前行的隨煩惱。於受用袈裟等僧伽物，或有居士邀請大眾僧或各別的出家人接受供養的時候，這類人都想前往第一個接受供養，這種意樂稱為趣向。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、前行</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科前行，說明前行的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若諸苾芻，於如是事最初前行，故名趣向前行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在眾多比丘中，對於施主供養的種種事，心中有欲及貪著，總是走在最先及在前面，這種意樂及行為，名為趣向前行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子十四、捨遠離軛</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十四科捨遠離軛，說明捨遠離軛的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p4971"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何捨遠離軛？謂於遠離邊際臥具、遠離眾惡人所習近似寂靜室，遠棄捨之，不生欲樂。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是捨遠離軛？行者不能得定的第十五種原因，是因為有捨遠離軛的隨煩惱。於遠離貪欲、粗劣的、下品的邊際臥具，於遠離各種惡法的住處，遠離眾惡人所習近之空林樹下的似寂靜室，對這些有助於修習止觀的資生具及處所，遠離棄捨，不生好樂。由此遠離善法軛的利益，不能使自己遠離不善的種種境界，使得不善諸欲數數生起，因此不容易得定。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　似寂靜室，據《瑜伽師地論略纂》卷16有兩種解釋：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、似寂靜室，指練苦處等，即房室遠離之處，若棄捨之，不去遠離之處，名遠離善軛。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、又解此是作婬欲處，眾惡所習近，名似寂靜室。應遠離之而不生欲樂，棄捨遠離此婬欲處似寂靜室之意，即不想遠離此婬欲處似寂靜室，不思修習善法，名遠離善軛。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子十五、於諸學處不甚恭敬</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十五科於諸學處不甚恭敬，說明於諸學處不甚恭敬的相狀。學處，就是戒，如出家比丘等應該學習的五篇七聚。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何於諸學處不甚恭敬？謂遭厄難，寧捨學處，不棄身命。志求身樂及與壽命，不能隨護所有學處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是於諸學處不甚恭敬？行者不能得定的第十六種原因，是因為有於諸學處不甚恭敬的隨煩惱，對各式各樣佛所制定的戒律，沒有很恭敬護持的心；於遭到危厄困難的時候，寧願捨棄所受的戒，也不放棄自己的身體、性命；寧願追求身體的快樂與得到壽命，不能隨順護持所受的戒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子十六、不顧沙門</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十六科不顧沙門，說明不顧沙門的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何不顧沙門？謂棄捨學處，好為退轉。或犯尸羅，行諸惡法，於內腐爛，廣說乃至實非梵行自稱梵行，況當希求沙門果證八支聖道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是不顧沙門？行者不能得定的第十七種原因，是因為有不顧沙門的隨煩惱。不顧慮到出家人應該要持戒，放棄捨離所應持守的戒律，由於歡喜諸欲而退失戒法；或者犯戒，造作種種惡法，內心有腐敗的貪瞋癡等常時活動，詳細說乃至沒有清淨的梵行，卻自稱有清淨的梵行，何況心裡根本沒有希望追求八支聖道，證初果乃至四果等沙門果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》或犯尸羅等者：此中諸義，如攝異門分別釋應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/84.htm#49522:64512">陵本八十四卷十四頁6396</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處所說的種種義理，如〈攝異門分〉卷84，2524頁所說應當了知。〈攝異門分〉說了很多關於不顧沙門的相貌。不顧沙門，是指外表行相上是出家人，卻犯了很多戒，不能如理作意，更何況修學聖道。這種不顧慮到自己應當自重自愛的沙門，有眾多隨煩惱，障礙自己不能得定。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子十七、活命出家</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十七科活命出家，說明活命出家的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何唯希活命不為涅槃而求出家？謂或為王之所逼迫而求出家，或為怨賊之所逼迫、或為債主之所逼切、或為恐怖之所逼切、或為財寶常所匱乏恐畏不活而求出家。不為自調、自靜、自般涅槃而求出家。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是希求能夠存活下去，不是為了涅槃而追求出家的修行者？行者不能得定的第十八種原因，是因為有唯希活命不為涅槃而求出家的隨煩惱。出家的動機是因為受到國王逼迫而去出家，不是自己願意出家、或是與他人有怨恨、或是有盜賊來逼迫、或是被債主之所逼迫急切想要逃避債務、或是財寶常所匱乏賺不到錢，常常三餐不繼恐怕不能活下去才來出家。這樣的人，不是為了要調伏自心的煩惱、追求眾苦的寂靜、不是想要成就自己證得聖道不再輪迴三界、不是想要成就圓滿的、不生不滅的無餘依涅槃而求出家。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p4972"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》不為自調自靜等者：調謂調伏，謂於煩惱。靜謂寂靜，謂於眾苦。證無餘依，名般涅槃。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　調是指調伏，就是調伏煩惱。靜是指寂靜，於生老病死等眾苦的寂靜。由調伏煩惱，證入無餘依涅槃，永不入生死，令生死眾苦寂靜，名為般涅槃。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、簡依處4　子一、有諂等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科簡依處，簡別十八種隨煩惱的依止處，分四科；第一科有諂等，說明有諂等隨煩惱的依止處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知此中，依同梵行而共止住有所違犯，發起最初四隨煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知在這十八種隨煩惱中，依止出家人同在一起修梵行而共住時候，發起最初的四種隨煩惱，包括有諂、有誑、有矯、有詐。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、無慚無愧</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科無慚無愧，說明無慚無愧隨煩惱的依止處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依增上戒有所違犯，當知發起無慚無愧。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依止於止惡行善的增上戒，有所犯戒時，應當知道已經有無慚無愧的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、不信等2　丑一、總標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科不信等，說明由不信等隨煩惱的依止處，分二科；第一科總標，總相標示出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依增上心及增上慧，當知發起始從不信，乃至惡慧諸隨煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依止增上心及增上慧，應當知道能發起不信、懈怠、忘念、不定，乃至惡慧等隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、別配</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別配，各別的配對。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中不信及與懈怠，依俱違犯；忘念、散亂，依增上心違犯而起；惡慧，依犯增上慧起。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這些隨煩惱當中，由不信三寶四諦、及由懈怠，喜歡睡眠不精進修行，這二種隨煩惱依增上心及增上慧有所違犯而生起。忘念，忘失正念，散亂，內心散亂，這二種隨煩惱依止增上心違犯而起，由此有種種的尋思散亂，不能常常在所緣境上數數憶念。惡慧就是邪見，沒有正確的智慧，依止違犯增上慧而生起惡慧。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子四、慢緩等2　丑一、不信等為增上</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科慢緩等，說明慢緩等隨煩惱的依止處，分二科；第一科不信等為增上，說明不信等為增上能生慢緩等隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不信、懈怠增上力故，當知發起慢緩、猥雜、趣向前行、捨遠離軛。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於不信三寶四諦及懈怠，這二種強大的增上力，應當知道會發起一、慢緩，不能勤修止觀，又不相信恭敬三寶有功德，也不能恭敬承事師長；二、猥雜，與在家眾及出家眾在一起雜住；三、趣向前行，有利養的時候，總是想在第一個走在前面接受供養；四、捨遠離軛，內心不能遠離邊際臥具，不能安貧樂道，不能遠離眾惡，不能安住在寂靜處。這都是因為有不信懈怠的緣故。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p4973"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、忘念等為增上</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科忘念等為增上，說明忘念等為增上於諸學處不甚恭敬等隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">忘念、亂心及與惡慧增上力故，當知發起於諸學處不甚恭敬、不顧沙門、唯希活命不為涅槃而求出家。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有忘念、亂心及有邪見的惡慧等隨煩惱的強大增上力為因，應當知道會發起對所制的戒不能深心恭敬，也不能作好一個出家人應作的事情，只是為了能夠活下去，不是為了真的要了脫生死，追求涅槃，而希求出家。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辛二、補特伽羅2　壬一、總標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科補特伽羅，約人說明禪定的障礙，分二科；第一科總標，總相標示出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有三種補特伽羅，依三處引諸隨煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有三種人，依止三種處所，會生起十八種隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬二、徵釋2　癸一、三種補特伽羅</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵釋，提出問題及解釋，分二科；第一科三種補特伽羅，說明三種人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何三種補特伽羅？一、依正法而出家者，二、在居家受用欲者，三、正法外而出家者。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪三種人依止三種處所，會生起諸隨煩惱？第一種是依止正法而出家的人，第二種是在家受用各式各樣色聲香味觸、男女諸欲的人，第三種是於正法以外而出家者，就是在外道出家，雖然也過著離欲的修行生活，可是不是佛法，是佛法以外的出家人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、三處引隨煩惱2　子一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科三處引隨煩惱，說明三種人依止三種處所能引生十八種隨煩惱，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何三處引隨煩惱？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是於三種處所而引生各式各樣的隨煩惱？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、釋3　丑一、依放逸處2　寅一、標能引</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分三科；第一科依放逸處，依止放逸的處所引發隨煩惱，又分二科；第一科標能引，標出第一種人依放逸處引發隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所謂最初補特伽羅，依放逸處引隨煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三種人中的第一種人，是依止放逸的處所引發隨煩惱。〈攝事分〉卷89說：於諸善品不樂勤修，於諸惡法心無防護故，名放逸。〈攝事分〉卷95說：若邪思惟，若邪尋思，若邪戲論，是名放逸；又廣說各種放逸的差別相。修行人若不能精進的斷惡生善，放逸而行，勢必引生隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、辨種類2　卯一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨種類，說明種類，分二科；第一科標，標示出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p4974"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復二種。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這一類人又可分為二種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、列2　辰一、依內</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出來，分二科；第一科依內，說明依止自身的一種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂或依內妄顯己德，為衣服等利養恭敬，自說己德勝過人法。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　放逸的情況有二種。第一種是依止著自己內身，虛妄的顯示自己有道力有功德，為了衣服、臥具、飲食等種種生活所須的資生利養、恭敬，自己讚歎自己很有道力、很有功德勝過他人、暗示他人自己已經得禪定或聖道了，由此引生有誑的隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、依他</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科依他，說明於他人以三業加以迫害。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或復依他諸有智者同梵行等，以身語業逼迫、加害、損惱、毀辱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於嫉妒有智慧者、或是對一起修清淨梵行的行者，用身業、語業乃至意業來逼迫對方、加害對方、損惱對方、毀辱對方，以此來得到恭敬利養。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、依耽欲處2　寅一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科依耽欲處，說明依止耽著於諸欲處引生隨煩惱，分二科；第一科標，標出第二種人依耽欲處引發隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知第二補特伽羅，依耽欲處引隨煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知三種人中的第二種人，是指在家受用諸欲者依止耽著色聲香味觸、男女等諸欲處，由此引生各式各樣的隨煩惱而犯戒，做出錯誤的事情。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼由耽著諸欲因緣，受用諸欲，依身語意行三惡行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這類在家人由於耽著色聲香味觸、男女諸欲的因緣，受用諸欲，由此依止身業、語業及意業，生起貪瞋癡三種惡行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑三、依邪行處3　寅一、標能引</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科依邪行處，說明依邪行處引生隨煩惱，分三科；第一科標能引，標出第三種人依邪行處引生隨煩惱，這是外道出家眾。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="74004:49560"></a>當知第三補特伽羅，依邪行處引隨煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種人是外道出家眾，依邪見的惡慧造作錯誤顛倒的行為，由此引生各式各樣的隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、辨種類2　卯一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨種類，說明邪行的種類，分二科；第一科標列，標示列舉出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">略有三種，謂隨逐遠離、隨逐憒鬧、隨逐學處起隨煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　要略而言外道出家眾有三種邪行的種類：一、隨逐應遠離導致染汙處的時候；二、或者是隨逐憒鬧雜居、有諍論的境界；三、或者是隨逐會違犯戒律的學處，由此生起隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p4975"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、隨釋3　辰一、隨逐遠離3　巳一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，隨著解釋，分三科；第一科隨逐遠離，說明隨逐遠離生起隨煩惱的相狀，又分三科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何隨逐遠離起隨煩惱？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱為隨逐遠離而生起隨煩惱？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、釋3　午一、住染汙</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分三科；第一科住染汙，說明內心住於煩惱的染汙相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂諸外道隨逐遠離所有臥具，而為五蓋覆蔽其心。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這類外道雖然隨逐遠離於寂靜處修行，受用邊際臥具，可是內心還是有貪欲、瞋恚、惛沈睡眠、掉舉惡作及疑五種煩惱蓋覆蒙蔽著內心，由此生起隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、住苦惱</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科住苦惱，說明住於痛苦煩惱的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或住於苦，領受身心諸苦惱故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有一種外道為求生天、為求解脫、或達到某種願望，採取折磨自己的苦行方式而修行，由此領受身心各種苦惱。認為吃苦就能了苦，不能了知應該斷除煩惱、不造業，才能真正了苦。這類人的苦行如坌灰拔髮、金雞獨立、投巖赴海，或日正當中曝曬在太陽底下，或裸形等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》或住於苦等者：謂如宿作因論者，於現法中極自苦行，說彼領受身心苦惱故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如執著宿作因論的外道，認為凡事都是過去生的業力所引生，與現在完全不相干，不注重現緣，不注重今生的努力，認為今生透過極端的苦行，就可以洗清過去的業力，不再受苦。因為於現生中極自苦行，所以領受身心苦惱。這種修行方式，執著單一因為諸苦生因，缺乏諸法由眾緣所生的正見，不能如實斷除煩惱，出離生死之苦，只是自找苦吃罷了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、無對治</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科無對治，沒有對治煩惱也會引發隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或復遠離煩惱對治，由離信等五種根故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或者遠離煩惱的對治，沒有以正法的方便對治煩惱，只是從表面上下功夫，以折磨身心的苦行為修行，不能找到苦的真正根源，遠離正信、正精進、正念、正定、正慧五種善根，白白吃苦卻不能了苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼由如是住染汙故，住苦惱故，無有對治能除染汙苦惱住故，是名隨逐遠離諸隨煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這類外道由於這樣住於五蓋等煩惱染汙的因緣，住於身苦心惱中，沒有正確的方法可以對治除去染汙的五蓋等煩惱及身心的痛苦，名為隨逐遠離諸隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p4976"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、隨逐憒鬧3　巳一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨逐憒鬧，說明隨逐憒鬧生起隨煩惱的相狀，分三科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何隨逐憒鬧起隨煩惱？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是隨逐憒鬧而生起各式各樣的隨煩惱？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂各別執異見、異欲相違言論，建立自品、他品差別，廣起忿、恨，乃至誑、諂。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這些隨逐憒鬧的外道出家人，執著各種異於佛法的見解思想、不想離欲、沒有斷煩惱的願望、持與佛法相違的言論，建立自論的品類、他論品類的差別，因此內心廣泛生起瞋忿、怨恨、覆藏自己的過失、惱怒、嫉妒、慳貪，乃至欺誑，或者是諂媚等隨逐憒鬧的各種隨煩惱。如本論卷7所說妄計清淨論等十六種外道論。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是名隨逐憒鬧諸隨煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上名為隨逐憒鬧諸隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》廣起忿恨乃至誑諂者：攝事分中說隨煩惱有多差別，謂忿、恨、覆、惱、嫉、慳、誑、諂，乃至廣說。今於此中唯取前八，如彼別釋應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/89.htm#49582:68193">陵本八十九卷七頁6738</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈攝事分〉卷89，2646頁中說隨煩惱有十種，包括忿、恨、覆、惱、嫉、慳、誑、諂，乃至詳細說還有各種隨煩惱。現在於此文中只取前八種，如那裡所各別解釋的應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、隨逐學處2　巳一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科隨逐學處，說明隨逐學處生起隨煩惱的相狀，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何隨逐學處起隨煩惱？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是隨逐戒定慧三種學處而生起各式各樣的隨煩惱？&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、釋3　午一、隨逐戒學</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分三科；第一科隨逐戒學，說明隨逐戒學的隨煩惱相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p4977"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂觀自他現行諸罪，無有羞恥，毀戒、穿戒，是名隨逐增上戒學諸隨煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在戒學方面，觀察自己、或他人現行種種犯戒的罪惡，沒有羞恥心，不覺得慚愧，毀犯上品的重戒而有毀戒的過失、或毀犯中下品的輕戒而有穿戒的過失，由此生起各種煩惱，稱為隨逐增上戒學諸隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、隨逐心學</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨逐心學，說明隨逐心學生起隨煩惱的相狀，這是指由禪定所生的隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有依止世間等至，於其下劣計自為勝，或於相似計自為勝，心生高舉，是名隨逐增上心學諸隨煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在定學方面，若有依止世間的禪定，於比自己下劣未得定者，生起高「慢」心，計度執著自己是殊勝的，或與自己相似已得世間禪定者相比，認為自己比較殊勝，而生起「過慢」的煩惱，名為隨逐增上心學諸隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、隨逐慧學</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科隨逐慧學，說明隨逐慧學生起隨煩惱的相狀，是指由修慧學所生的隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若少聽聞，不能觀察所有善法，是名隨逐增上慧學諸隨煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在慧學方面，由於很少聽聞佛法，沒有智慧也不學習，不能深入觀察什麼是善法，什麼是不善法，稱為隨逐增上慧學諸隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、釋邪行2　卯一、標異名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋邪行，說明錯誤的行為，分二科；第一科標異名，標出邪行不同的名稱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="34406:49593"></a>如是一切，總略說名非法之行、不平等行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如是這一切，總相說或要略說，不善的邪行稱為非法之行，邪行之因所得的惡果名不平等行。非法就是不善；不平等行，指因與果不平等，例如造惡因想要得樂果，或者是不平等因論，名不平等行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋差別，解釋邪行的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="64466:49595"></a>由非善義，名非法行；非愛果義，名不平等行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於不是善法的境界，所作的事，不是與善心所相應，而是與煩惱心所相應，稱為非法行，這是從因而說；以非法行為因所得不可愛果的境界，稱為不平等行，這是從果而說。外道行苦行，雖然能於遠離處依邊際臥具修行，可是仍然有五蓋覆蔽其心，在戒定慧三學方面，生起各式各樣的煩惱。由於毀戒，於禪定生起高慢心，又不能聽聞佛法，當然不能得到可愛的果報，這樣稱為不平等行。如〈本地分‧菩薩地〉卷43，1463頁所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">己二、辨解脫2　庚一、舉十遍處3　辛一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨解脫，說明解脫的相狀，分二科；第一科舉十遍處，舉出十遍處說明解脫，又分三科；第一科標，標出十遍處能為五事。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，若觀行者修十遍處，能為五事。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，若是修習三乘觀行的人，修十遍處能有五種功德。在〈本地分‧三摩呬多地〉卷12，412頁有詳細說明十遍處的修行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辛二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p4978"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等為五？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪五種功德？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辛三、釋2　壬一、辨作業5　癸一、能引化事變事神通</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科辨作業，辨明十遍處的作用，又分五科；第一科能引化事變事神通，修習前八遍處能引發化事、變事諸聖神通。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂由修習地遍處等乃至白遍處故，便能引發化事、變事諸聖神通。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於行者修習地水火風、青黃赤白等八遍處，就能引發令色物由無而有的「化事」、及令已有的色物轉變的「變事」等諸多聖人不可思議的神通之事。如〈本地分‧三摩呬多地〉卷12，413頁說：「八色遍處，善清淨故，能引賢聖勝解神通，及於諸事轉變神通，如其勝解，隨所轉變，皆能成就。又能變作金銀等物，堪有所用。」諸聖是簡別不共於凡夫、外道的神通。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼說成辦前八遍處故，能引發化事、變事？《瑜伽師地論略纂》卷16窺基大師說：因為前八遍處修成功，於境色中得自在故，因此能引發化事、變事。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、能引往還無礙神通</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科能引往還無礙神通，修空遍處能引發往還無礙的神通。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又由修習空無邊處一切處故，便能引發往還無礙諸聖神通。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又由於修習空無邊處，修一切法都是空的，觀一切色法都沒有障礙；所以能夠引發往還無礙，要去那裡都沒有障礙的諸聖神通。若有神足通，能夠穿石，也能夠穿牆越壁，飛山走海往還無礙。如〈本地分‧三摩呬多地〉卷12，413頁說：「由空遍處善清淨故，隨其所欲皆轉成空。」</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼說成辦空遍處故，能引發往還無礙神通？《瑜伽師地論略纂》卷16窺基大師說：因為得空無邊處定時，沒有色法的障礙，因此能引往還無礙。此往還無礙神通，也是依四禪。但要先得空遍處，除去色的障礙，再入四靜慮，施展往還無礙的神通。雖然也有主張不得空遍處等，而得往還無礙，這不是增勝者語，因為定色的障礙未盡除故，有些色處仍有障礙。此處據勝而言得空遍處才能於一切色處無礙。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸三、能引無諍等勝功德</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科能引無諍等勝功德，修識遍處能引發無諍等殊勝功德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又由修習識無邊處一切處故，便能引發無諍、願智、無礙解等諸勝功德。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又由於修習識無邊處，一切法不離識，都是識所變現，觀心識遍滿虛空上下左右一切處，由此就能引發無諍三昧、願智三昧、四無礙解三昧等種種功德。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如〈本地分‧三摩呬多地〉卷12，413頁說：「由識遍處善清淨故，便能引發無諍、願智、無礙解等諸勝功德。」</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼說成辦識遍處故，能引發無諍願智等功德？《瑜伽師地論略纂》卷16窺基大師說：諸功德法，都是心識的功德，都是心法；由識處得自在故，即如識於境得自在。得識遍處後依第四靜慮，引發此無諍願智等功德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸四、能辦上處解脫</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科能辦上處解脫，修十遍處能夠成辦往上解脫的功德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又即由此識無邊處遍處成滿，便能成辦無所有處解脫，及非想非非想處解脫。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又由於有識無邊處的識遍滿一切上下左右，便能成辦無所有處解脫，及非想非非想處解脫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸五、能證滅受想定</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科能證滅受想定，修十遍處能夠證入滅盡定。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又即由此成滿因故，便能證入想受滅解脫，最勝住所攝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又由於此識無邊處成滿的原因，便能證入想受滅解脫，是最殊勝的聖住所攝。〈本地分‧菩薩地〉卷38，1258頁說：「由諸如來多住無上無等三住，謂：聖住、天住、梵住故，名住最勝。當知：此中，空、無願、無相住，及滅盡定住，是名聖住。四種靜慮、四無色定，是名天住。四種無量，是名梵住。」想受滅解脫即滅盡定住，滅盡定是四種聖住所攝，所以此處說最勝住所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬二、明邊際</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明邊際，說明十遍處的邊際。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又由識無邊處故，無邊無量遍滿行轉，是故此上不立遍處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又由於識無邊處，沒有邊際，也沒有數量，遍滿五蘊及器世間諸行而轉，所以在心識以上就不安立遍處了。這是說明十遍處，為什麼不安立無所有，為什麼不安立非想非非想處，因為無所有處及非想非非想處也不離識。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽師地論略纂》卷16窺基大師說：觀識於無邊無量遍滿行轉，修此識無邊處，作無量無邊觀行，無邊觀行於此處究竟故，因此更不依無所有處及非想非非想處立遍處、勝處。這是總結前文由識處成辦故，便能引發無諍、願智、無礙解等諸勝功德。關於功德，如《顯揚聖教論》卷20（大正31，578c15～579a1）功德決擇所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p4979"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">庚二、顯諸解脫2　辛一、彼清淨道</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯諸解脫，說明各種解脫，分二科；第一科彼清淨道，說明八解脫的清淨道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">勝處、遍處是諸解脫能清淨道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八勝處與十遍處是使八解脫能夠更加清淨的方法，能使八解脫究竟圓滿。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽師地論略纂》卷16說：此處以八解脫為果，以八勝處與十遍處為前方便。《大乘阿毘達磨雜集論》卷13說：「依解脫故造修，由勝處故起方便，由遍處故成滿。若於彼得成滿，即於解脫究竟。」這是依解脫斷障故。這種說法與聲聞乘的薩婆多部不同，薩婆多部說：解脫唯是因，於最初修習，要先依解脫一分取得斷障，遍處唯果，末後修故；勝處通於因果，在解脫之後，遍處之前修故。此處文中以解脫為果，勝處遍處為因，不同於《成實論》所說。彼《成實論》卷12說遍處為因，解脫（主張八解脫中說漏盡滅，非入滅定）為果，勝處通因果，於最後修。又《大乘阿毘達磨雜集論》約解脫究竟時而說，必定要成就八勝處及十遍處，解脫才能圓滿，以解脫為果故。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又據《瑜伽論記》卷17說：「解脫有二種。一、如量智中作入解脫觀，指內有色外觀色等；二、如理智中作解脫觀，觀前七種解脫所觀之境平等真如。若依如量智中作解脫觀，即八解脫而為初，次修勝處、後修遍處，如本論前文所說。毘曇（有部等）取此次第說三種功德。若依如理智中作解脫觀，即先修遍處，次修勝處後修解脫。再依此如理智中作解脫觀的道理，因此說勝處遍處是諸解脫能清淨道。不同成實論所說十遍處唯因，解脫唯果，勝處通因果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》勝處遍處等者：本地分說：修觀行者，先於所緣思惟勝解；次能制伏；既於制伏得自在已，後即於此遍一切處，如其所欲而作勝解；是故此三如是次第。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/12.htm#49616:9774">陵本十二卷八頁995</a>）又說：譬如世間瓦鐵金師，初和泥等，未善調練，解脫位亦爾。如善調練，勝處位亦爾。如調練已，隨欲轉變，遍處位亦爾。此所說義，如彼應知。謂由勝處、遍處，令先所緣思惟勝解，轉清淨故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈本地分〉說：修觀行的人，先對於所緣境，包括青、黃、赤、白，色少、色多，乃至空、識，思惟以後，得到強而有力的勝解；其次能夠修制伏想，於所緣色法能夠使青變黃、黃變赤、淨色變不淨色、少色變多色、多色變少、好變惡、惡變好等，能夠控制、伏除，可以隱蔽它，也可以轉變它，有這種自在力又不起增上慢，名為有制伏想，成就八勝處，這時觀想的力量就很強了；既於所緣制伏得自在已，後即於此所緣觀想遍一切處，盡虛空、遍法界，上下左右旁邊，如其內心所想的而作勝解，成就十遍處；因此這三種修法有此先後次第。如〈本地分‧三摩呬多地〉卷12，413頁所說。</span></span></span></div>
