<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、依思惟過去美好的事情而令心掉動高舉、或心向外攀緣色聲香味觸而流動散亂、或有錯誤的見解、或聽聞外道邪見相應的惡法、或有暴惡的語言、或有暴惡的行為，只好樂聽聞佛法及思惟佛法，不修禪定，心的自制力不足，使心流散動亂；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、由過去時常串習散亂的作用力，由此作用所持令心流動散亂。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由這三種原因，導致修心清淨行的比丘生起散亂尋思。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、保著內身</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科保著內身，說明保著內身的隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">保著內身者，由於生死無厭患門。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　保著內身的行者，由於對生死沒有厭離心，也不知生死的過失災患，因此特別顧惜、保護、愛著自己的身體，由此不能捍勞忍苦精勤修行而障礙修定。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子四、保著外境</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科保著外境，說明保著外境的情況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">保著外境者，於未來境由欣樂門。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　保護執著外境的行者，由於對於未來的色聲香味觸、財色名食睡、名聞利養等境界還有很多的希求及欣樂，心向外追求不能內攝於清淨所緣，由此障礙修定。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p4991"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬二、明彼對治2　癸一、舉能對治4　子一、正知作意</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明彼對治，說明四種隨煩惱的對治方法，分二科；第一科舉能對治，舉出能對治四種隨煩惱的方法，又分四科；第一科正知作意，以正知作意來對治犯戒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知此中，為欲對治初隨煩惱故，修一作意，謂正知作意。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當知道這其中，為了要對治最初一種毀犯禁戒的隨煩惱，修習一種作意，即正知作意。由正知作意，隨時正確覺知自己的身語意三業是否如法如律，由此便能防止因忘失正念而毀犯禁戒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、稱順彼所緣等作意2　丑一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科稱順彼所緣等作意，修習稱順彼所緣等作意，能對治第二種散亂尋思的隨煩惱，分二科；第一科標，標出三種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">為欲對治第二隨煩惱故，修三作意。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為了對治由三種門引生的第二種散亂尋思的隨煩惱，應當修習三種作意。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出三種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂稱順彼所緣作意；了別彼相，能對治彼尋思作意；彼所依心調練作意。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對治第二種散亂尋思隨煩惱的三種作意包括：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、稱順彼所緣作意，若於所緣的過去境不知無常，則修無常觀令知無常，若於所緣的過去境生起貪欲則修不淨觀對治；若於所緣的過去境生起瞋恚則修慈悲觀對治；若於所緣的過去境散亂過度則修數息觀對治；若於所緣的過去境生起愚痴則修緣起觀對治；若於所緣的過去境生起我慢則修界差別觀對治，如是等隨類修習稱合隨順彼所緣的對治作意，名稱順彼所緣作意；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、了別掉舉等相的生起因緣及過患，修習能對治掉舉等尋思的作意，稱為了別彼相，能對治彼尋思作意，如修習九心住等定地作意能對治掉舉、散亂，修習緣起正見等增上慧能對治惡見、惡聞，修習增上戒能對治惡語、惡行，修習止觀能對治唯樂聞思散亂；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、於前二種長時串習散亂難除，修習九心住令心內住等，遠離散亂尋思，名彼所依心調練作意。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、分析積聚作意</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科分析積聚作意，修習分析積聚作意能對治第三種保著內身的隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">為欲對治第三隨煩惱故，應修分析積聚作意。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為了對治第三種保著內身的隨煩惱，應當修習界分別觀，分析內身的色法，是由地水火風等積聚而成，心法是由受想行識積聚而成，觀身無實、無我，於身遠離有情想，或如《金剛經》所說將此身碎為微塵作微塵觀，就可以對治保護愛著內身的隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子四、不淨作意</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科不淨作意，修習外境的不淨作意能第四種保著外境。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">為欲對治第四隨煩惱故，應當修習不淨作意。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為了對治第四種保著外境的隨煩惱，應當修習不淨觀，對治內心於外境的貪著。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p4992"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》修三作意等者：唯樂聞思散亂，三為所依。一、依掉舉，二、依流散，三、依惡見、惡聞、惡語、惡行。修三作意，如次能為對治應知。言稱順彼所緣作意者，謂有貪行者，修不淨觀，於相稱緣安住其心。本地分中已說其相。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/26.htm#49751:22011">陵本二十六卷十七頁2220</a>）由是下說：第二作意修習、多修習故，能斷保著內身、外境二種貪欲。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若是唯獨好樂聽聞思惟而有散亂，這是以三種因緣為所依止而生。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、依掉舉，因親屬尋思、國土尋思、不死尋思、或隨順憶念過去所經歷戲笑歡娛所行之事，心生諠動騰躍之性；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、依流散，於身外五種妙欲諸雜亂相所有尋思隨煩惱中，及於身外所緣境中，縱心流散；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、依惡邪見、惡聞、惡語、惡行，三業不寂境而令心散亂。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若修習稱順彼所緣作意、了別彼相能對治彼尋思作意、彼所依心調練作意三種作意，依次第能對治這三種散亂的因緣應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所謂稱順彼所緣作意，是指貪心較重的行者，應修習不淨觀；於瞋心較重的行者應修慈悲觀；癡心較重的行者應修十二緣起；對於慢心較重的行者，應修界分別觀；散亂尋伺重者應修數息觀，於能對治相，稱合所緣安住其心，由此令心清淨，名稱順彼緣作意。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷26，905頁已說其中的相狀。如〈聲聞地〉說：彼比丘若唯有貪行，應於不淨緣安住於心，如是名為於相稱緣安住其心等。因此下文說於第二稱順彼所緣作意修習、多修習故，能斷除保著內身、外境二種貪欲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、顯所對治5　子一、忘念</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯所對治，顯示正知等作意所對治的煩惱，分五科；第一科忘念，修第一種作意能對治忘失正念的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又初作意修習、多修習故，能斷忘念。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又修習第一種正知作意，由於修習、及多修習的因緣，能斷除忘失正念的過失，不會毀犯淨戒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、貪欲</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科貪欲，修第二種作意能對治貪欲的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第二作意修習、多修習故，能斷保著內身、外境二種貪欲。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由第二種稱順彼緣作意修習、多修習的緣故，能夠斷除保著內身、外境的二種貪欲。稱順彼緣作意有多種，這是專指不淨觀而言。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、散亂2　丑一、惡見等散亂</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科散亂，說明散亂的對治，分二科；第一科惡見等散亂，修第三種作意能對治惡見等散亂的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第三作意修習、多修習故，能斷惡見等所有散亂。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種了別彼相能對治彼尋思作意修習、多修習的緣故，能夠斷除掉舉、流散、惡見、惡聞、惡語、惡行等所引生的散亂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、患習勢力任持散亂</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科患習勢力任持散亂，修第四種作意能對治先所串習勢力任持散亂的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第四作意修習、多修習故，能斷先所串習勢力任持所有散亂。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由第四種彼所依心調練作意，就是九心住，這種定的作意修習、多修習故，能斷除過去常常串習勢力所任持的散亂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子四、於身淨有情想</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科於身淨有情想，修第五種作意能對治於身淨有情想的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第五作意修習、多修習故，能斷於身淨有情想。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由第五種分析積聚作意修習、多修習的緣故，能夠斷除自身是清淨的有情想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子五、四種婬相應貪</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科四種婬相應貪，修第六種作意能對治四種婬相應貪的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p4993"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第六作意修習、多修習故，能斷四貪。所謂色貪、觸貪、形貪，及承事貪。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六種不淨作意修習、多修習的緣故，能夠斷除樂見膚白色淨等的顯色貪、樂觸柔軟細滑等的妙觸貪、喜好高矮胖瘦等的形色貪，及愛著殷勤奉事等的承事貪等四種煩惱。〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷26說：修習外身不淨時，若觀青瘀、膿爛、變壞、膖脹、食噉作意思惟，能對治行者於有情身上青黃赤白等「顯色貪」，令心清淨；若於變赤作意思惟，能對治行者愛著有情身形雄偉曼妙等「形色貪」，令心清淨；若於其骨、若於其鎖、若於骨鎖作意思惟，能對治行者歡喜觸對柔軟細滑的「妙觸貪」，令心清淨；若於散壞作意思惟，能對治行者貪著他人代勞做事的「承事貪」，令心清淨。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷17解釋略有不同：「依小乘解作青瘀觀能治色貪，貪紅白等色；骨鎖觀除去觸貪；作骨節分離觀除去形容貪；作死屍觀除去承事貪。」</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辛二、定地清淨攝2　壬一、正定</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科定地清淨攝，說明定地清淨所攝的差別，分二科；第一科正定，說明正定清淨的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是作意修習為依，斷隨煩惱，心觸正定，證得近分、根本勝定，又能證得有喜、離喜、清淨安樂。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依止修習前文所說六種作意，斷除以上所說的毀犯禁戒、散亂尋思、保著內身、保著外境等四種隨煩惱，令心可以觸及正定，證得諸禪的近分定、或初禪乃至四禪等根本勝定，又能證得有喜，初禪及二禪都是有喜；離喜，三禪的離喜妙樂；清淨安樂，就是四禪的捨念清淨等諸禪所生的功德。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷17對這段文提出五種解釋：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、能證得有喜離喜清淨安樂者得下三定。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、又解，初、二定名有喜第三定名離喜，第四定名安樂清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、又解，第三定名離喜安樂，四定已上乃至非想名為清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、又解，四定已上乃至非想名安樂清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、又解，第三定已上總名離喜。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》有喜離喜清淨安樂者：四靜慮中，初二靜慮名有喜安樂，第三靜慮名離喜安樂，第四靜慮名清淨安樂。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四靜慮中，初靜慮及第二靜慮稱為有喜安樂，第三靜慮稱為離喜安樂，第四靜慮，名為清淨安樂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬二、正知2　癸一、總標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科正知，正確的了知有情無常性，及諸行無常性，分二科；第一科總標，總相標出正知的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又依如是正定心故，如實了知上地有情無常性，及諸行無常性。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又依止這種清淨的正定心，能如實了知生到色界、或無色界上地的有情還是無常性，以及五蘊或器世間有為諸行的無常性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、別釋2　子一、了知有情無常性</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別釋，各別解釋，分二科；第一科了知有情無常性，說明了知有情的無常性的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何了知有情無常性？謂得天眼，清淨過人，見諸有情，乃至廣說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼行者得正定心，能如實了知有情是無常的？這是因為行者依止禪定，證得天眼通，內心清淨，超過一般人的境界，可以看到有情過去多生以來，不斷死、不斷生，乃至未來也會死、也會生，或看到有情前一生是畜生，這一生是人，下一生是欲界天、色界天等，乃至詳細說有各式各樣的情況。這段文如〈本地分‧思所成地〉卷18，670頁說：「復有或善男子或善女人，為性聰慧，獲得天眼；用此天眼見諸有情死時生時，如經廣說，乃至生在大那落迦中。」</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》乃至廣說者：謂彼有情死時、生時、妙色、惡色、若劣、若勝等，是名廣說應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　證得天眼通的行者，能看到有情，死時的情形、生時的情形、外表的妙色或是惡色，受用的果報是下劣、或殊勝等種種差別相，稱為廣說應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、了知諸行無常性</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科了知諸行無常性，說明了知諸行無常性的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p4994"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何了知諸行無常性？謂能隨入未來、過去、現在作意緣生智故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼行者得正定心，能如實了知五蘊或器世間有為諸行無常性？這是因為行者得正定心後，能隨所欲憶念過去、思惟未來、及入於現在五蘊或器世間有為諸行都是眾緣所生，此有故彼有，此生故彼生，如是因如是果等，由此作意通達緣生的智慧。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論手記》卷4說：得緣生智者，是指了達緣生諸法，橫如幻化無實我。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》隨入未來過去現在作意緣生智者：謂於三世諸行如理作意，知唯緣生，能正對治前際無知、後際無知、前後際無知故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　隨入未來過去現在作意緣生智就是對於三世，過去、現在、未來的五蘊或器世間的有為諸行，了知一切法都是因緣所生，能夠正確對治執著前際，即過去世的五蘊或器世間的諸行為我我所的愚癡無知；後際無知，對治執著未來世的五蘊或器世間的諸行為我我所的愚癡；前後際無知，對治執著現在世的五蘊或器世間的諸行為我我所的愚癡。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辛三、依處清淨攝3　壬一、標依處</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科依處清淨攝，依處清淨所攝的差別，分三科；第一科標依處，標示出依處的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此隨身念依於三處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此經所說隨身念，修身念住的時候，主要依止於三處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬二、列三種</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列三種，列出三種學處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂依增上心、增上慧學修治業地，依增上心學處，依增上慧學處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　修身念住所依止的三處，第一處是依止增上心學的奢摩他，增上慧學的毗鉢舍那修習禪觀對治的業地，就是修習定慧的資糧法，如〈聲聞地〉卷22所說自他圓滿善法欲、戒根律儀食知量、悎寤正知住善友、聞思無障捨莊嚴等十四種資糧；或依止增上心的奢摩他學處，修習定地作意降伏煩惱，或依止增上慧的毗鉢舍那學處，修習觀慧斷除煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬三、釋所為</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋所為，解釋三處的功能。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">為欲斷除所餘諸結，修念住等所有一切菩提分法之所依止。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這三處是為了漸次斷除所餘的微細煩惱，必須修習四念住、四正勤、五根、五力、七菩提分、八聖道分等所有菩提分法所依止的定資糧，由此定資糧具足能成就奢摩他及毗鉢舍那。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》增上心學增上慧學修治業地者：謂成就戒律儀、根律儀，乃至沙門莊嚴。如是一切勝資糧法，能為作意初修業者，及淨煩惱初修業者所依止處，是故名彼修治業地。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　增上心學增上慧學修治業地，是指成就戒律儀、根律儀，乃至沙門莊嚴等世間及出世間二道資糧。這一切殊勝的資糧法，能為作意初修業者，即初修定地作意者，及淨煩惱初修業者，即依所得未到地定等修習觀慧斷煩惱者所依止處，所以稱為彼增上心學、增上慧學修治業地。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是於作意初修業者，及淨煩惱初修業者？本論卷28說：云何於作意初修業者？謂初修業補特伽羅，安住一緣，勤修作意，乃至未得所修作意，未能觸證心一境性。云何淨煩惱初修業者？謂已證得所修作意，於諸煩惱欲淨其心，發起攝受正勤修習了相作意，名淨煩惱初修業者。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辛四、不共清淨攝2　壬一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科不共清淨攝，說明不共清淨所攝的差別 ，分二科；第一科標，標出不共外道沙門、婆羅門的因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p4995"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由三因緣，不與一切外道沙門、婆羅門共。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛法裡面所修的止觀都是清淨的，有三種因緣不與一切外道的出家眾及在家的婆羅門一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬二、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋不共的三種因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂於修治業地資糧圓滿故；於奢摩他聚無有愛味故；於般涅槃愛樂隨逐心，非煩惱火所生處故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛法裡面所修的止觀，有三種與外道不共之處：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一是對於修治業地的資糧很圓滿，外道不一定具足這些資糧而得定；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二是對於所得的奢摩他聚，各種禪定都沒有愛戀味著，而外道於所得禪定經常生起愛著；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三佛法裡面所得的止觀是由於對出離三界生死入不生不滅的涅槃有愛樂隨逐之心而修，涅槃不是有為的煩惱火所生處，而外道以為禪定就是涅槃，追求生到色界四禪天，或者是無色界四空天，這二種處所還在三界生死中，還是煩惱火所生之處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辛五、不共果清淨攝3　壬一、資糧圓滿2　癸一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科不共果清淨攝，說明不共果清淨所攝的差別 ，分三科；第一科資糧圓滿，說明資糧圓滿為依能得果清淨，又分二科；第一科標，標出四果清淨所依。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又此修念資糧圓滿為依止故，四果清淨。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又佛法中修習正念的資糧，以增上心及增上慧的修治業地資糧法修習圓滿為依止，能證得四種清淨的結果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋四果清淨的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂處聚落，世法所生煩惱不染；</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四果清淨的第一種是：雖然處在聚落，世間的利衰毀譽稱譏苦樂八法所引生的煩惱不會染汙自己的心。智顗大師《摩訶止觀》卷5說：「止是壁定，八風惡覺所不能入。」如果止觀的資糧法修習圓滿，即使在人事紛擾的聚落處，也不為世間興衰所生的煩惱所動搖。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》世法所生煩惱不染者：本地分說有八世法。謂得、不得、若譽、若毀、稱、譏、苦、樂。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/02.htm#49793:1481">陵本二卷十五頁160</a>）不依彼法而生煩惱，名彼煩惱不染。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈本地分〉說有八種世間法。包括：得，就是利，凡有益於我，都稱為利；不得是衰，凡有減損於我，都稱為衰；若譽是背後的善言讚譽；若毀是背後的毀謗；稱是當面的稱道己善；譏是當面的譏笑誹謗；苦的境界及樂的境界。這是人類都必然經歷的境界。如〈本地分‧意地〉卷2，70頁所說。若是止觀的資糧修習圓滿，不因世法動搖而生煩惱，名為彼煩惱不染。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">處阿練若，空閑所生煩惱不染；</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種資糧圓滿的清淨果是：在寂靜處修習止觀的時候，內心不為色聲香味觸、貪瞋癡男女十相、欲恚害等八種尋思、及貪欲等五蓋的煩惱染著內心。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p4996"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》空閑所生煩惱不染者：謂閑居時，或於塵霧，或昏夜分，見大雲氣，聞震雷音；或逢雹雨師子虎豹；或遭凶猾竊劫抄虜；或遇非人來相嬈逼；便生驚怖，身毛為豎。或至晝分，於彼去來奇妙親友，發依耽嗜所有尋思。謂欲尋思，如經廣說，乃至家世相應尋思。如本地分。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/18.htm#49796:15232">陵本十八卷八頁1557</a>）是名空閑所生煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　居住在阿蘭若寂靜處時，或是於有灰塵煙霧時，或是在黃昏、夜晚的時候，看到很多的烏雲、山嵐濕氣，聽到震耳的雷音；或遇到下冰雹暴雨、師子、老虎、野豹；或遭遇凶悍狡猾的盜竊搶劫抄襲俘虜、或遇非人來相嬈亂逼害；由此生起驚慌恐怖，渾身汗毛豎立，起雞皮疙瘩。或者是白天的時候，對於來來往往的奇妙親友，發起歡喜愛味耽溺執著的所有尋思，就是欲尋思，如經上有詳細的說明，乃至對家勢相應尋思。如〈本地分‧思所成地〉卷18，654頁所說。以上是名空閑所生煩惱。若是止觀的資糧修習圓滿，不會被這些寂靜處所生的煩惱染汙自心。　</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">處阿練若，聚落所生煩惱不染；</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種資糧圓滿的清淨果是：處阿蘭若於寂靜處由人非人等所生的煩惱，或處聚落於憒鬧處世間八法所生的煩惱，由此二處所生的煩惱都不會染著他。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》聚落所生煩惱不染者：本地分說：於求財者深修厭毀；於諸城邑交遊等處，了知其初、了知過患、了知出離，亦能了知趣出離行。生彼因緣，說名為初。無常、眾苦、變壞法性，是名過患。欲貪調伏斷除超越，名為出離。聖八支道，名趣出離行。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/18.htm#49798:15439">陵本十八卷十四頁1575</a>）其義應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈本地分〉說：對於求財這件事行者深心修習厭離、毀壞之想，了知這些身外之物於戒定慧毫無所益、反生禍害、不值得追求、應當遠離、也知道如何遠離；對於到城市、交友遊逛等處，知道是生起內心染著的因緣、知道這些俗事會生起種種的過失災患、障礙修習止觀、知道應該出離到聚落由求財或交遊等所生的煩惱、也能夠了知趣向出離煩惱的方法。生起煩惱的因緣，稱為初。財物及名聞利養、親友眷屬等都是無常、能引生種種的苦惱、具有變壞法性，將來勢必變化破壞，這些有為法之無常、苦、變壞的法性，就是過患。內心的欲貪煩惱能夠調伏不令現行、或者是斷除種子、或者是超越煩惱證得圓滿的無漏聖道，稱為出離。聖人所說的八正道，是趣向出離的方法，稱為趣出離行。如〈本地分‧思所成地〉卷18，660頁所說的義理應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於二處所，不能堪忍淋漏等苦煩惱不染。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四種資糧圓滿的清淨果是：於阿蘭若寂靜處或於聚落憒鬧處二種處所，不能堪受忍耐房舍破漏有淋雨、漏雨等苦惱或有蚊蟲等螫咬的煩惱，這些煩惱不能染著自心。行者若修止觀的資糧圓滿，一心修習止觀，對於所處外境之不如意，心不攀緣、不介意、能忍苦為道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬二、定無愛味果2　癸一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科定無愛味果，說明不共外道的於定無愛味果，分二科；第一科標，標示五果清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">奢摩他聚無有愛味為依止故，五果清淨。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者若於所得各式各樣的禪定，沒有愛味執著以此為依止，能得到五種非常清淨的果報。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋五果清淨的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p4997"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂四種清淨靜慮，及寂靜解脫。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五果清淨是指證得初禪到四禪等四種清淨的靜慮，及空無邊處定、識無邊處定、無所有處定、乃至非想非非想處定四種無色定的寂靜解脫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》寂靜解脫者：謂無色定應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　寂靜解脫是指四無色定應當了知。證得四無色定，內心遠離欲界欲及色界色的繫縛，相對於下二界，進入深定，內心寂靜，因此名寂靜解脫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬三、愛樂涅槃果2　癸一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科愛樂涅槃果，說明不共外道的愛樂涅槃果，分二科；第一科標，標出九果清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於般涅槃愛樂隨逐，心非煩惱火所生處為依止故，九果清淨。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者以涅槃為上首，追求愛樂的是遠離生死輪迴的煩惱，證入不生不滅的涅槃界，心以清淨寂靜為依止處，煩惱動亂的火在這種清淨寂靜無雜染處是無法生起的，由此能得到九種清淨的結果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋九果清淨的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂初三果及六神通。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　九果清淨是指初果、二果、三果等初三果及天眼通、天耳通、神足通、他心通、宿命智、漏盡通等六神通。此處沒有說證得四果，僅說六神通，但只有四果的阿羅漢才能證得漏盡通，由此可知事實上能證得四種聖道果及六種神通。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">庚三、略攝要義2　辛一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科略攝要義，要略歸納《隨身念經》的重要意義，分二科；第一科標，標出五種清淨所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此隨身念，當知五種清淨所攝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡所說的隨身念，隨身心安住的正念，應當知道是由五種清淨所攝持的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辛二、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋五種清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂不定地清淨故、定地清淨故、攝清淨故、不共清淨故、不共果清淨故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《隨身念經》的重點就是不定地清淨、定地清淨、攝清淨、不共清淨、不共果清淨五種清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、不定地清淨，由六種作意能夠對治四種煩惱，雖然沒有得定也可以清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、定地清淨，得到禪定，又知道有情的無常性，一切有為法的無常性，不於禪定生愛味，可以獲得定地清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、攝清淨，是指三種依處清淨，於修止觀的資糧法、增上心學處清淨、增上慧學處清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、不共清淨，於修止觀的資糧法圓滿、於奢摩他沒有愛味、於般涅槃愛樂隨逐，心非煩惱火所生處為依止，故是不共外道的清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、不共果清淨，依前三種不共外道的清淨因緣，能得到如前面所說的四種果、五種果，及九種果的清淨。這些都是不共於外道的功德。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是《隨身念經》的重點。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》五種清淨所攝等者：前說作意能治四隨煩惱，不定地清淨所攝。證得有喜、離喜、清淨安樂，了知有情諸行無常，定地清淨所攝。依於三處，攝清淨所攝。由三因緣，不共清淨所攝。所餘諸相，不共果清淨所攝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前面說六種作意，能夠對治毀犯禁戒、散亂尋思、保著內身、保著外境四種隨煩惱，是屬於不定地清淨所攝。得到禪定的人，證得有喜的初禪、二禪、離喜的三禪、清淨的四禪，都是安樂的境界，有喜安樂、離喜安樂、清淨安樂，了知有情及五蘊器世間諸行都是無常的，這是定地清淨所攝。依止三處包括增上心、增上慧修治業地即止觀的資糧、增上心學處、增上慧學處，這三處屬於攝清淨所攝。由三種因緣，包括修治業地資糧圓滿，於奢摩他聚無有愛故，於般涅槃愛樂隨逐，心非煩惱火所生處，不去追逐三界殊勝的人天果報，這些是不共於外道的清淨所攝。其餘的諸相，包括四果清淨、五果清淨及九果清淨，都是不共於外道的果清淨所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p4998"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">庚四、釋彼經名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科釋彼經名，解釋《隨身念經》的名義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又隨逐身轉故，彼所攝受故，名隨身念。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這部經為什麼稱為《隨身念經》？因為依經中所說作意、了知無常、三種依處、不共清淨、不共清淨果所得五種清淨，能隨逐行者的身心現前運轉，行者的身心、由五種清淨的正念所攝，稱為《隨身念經》。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">己二、摩訶俱瑟祉羅經2　庚一、標所釋經</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科摩訶俱瑟祉羅經，引釋《摩訶俱瑟祉羅經》，分二科；第一科標所釋經，標出所解釋的經名。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，當釋摩訶俱瑟祉羅經。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，應當解釋《摩訶俱瑟祉羅經》。這部經也稱為《大俱祉羅經》，這是一位大比丘的法號，以他的法號來為這部經命名。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷17說：摩訶俱瑟祉羅，就是舊說摩訶俱絺羅。摩訶是大；俱瑟祉，中文翻為肚；羅，中文翻為持，全文即大肚持。大肚是大藏義，這是指舍利弗的舅舅長爪梵志。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　關於此經可以參考《中阿含經》卷58（第211經）〈大拘絺羅經〉（大正1，790b3～792c3）。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">庚二、廣顯彼義3　辛一、二種解脫2　壬一、總標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣顯彼義，廣泛說明《摩訶俱瑟祉羅經》的義理，分三科；第一科二種解脫，說明二種解脫，又分二科；第一科總標列，總相標示列出二種解脫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">有二解脫。一、慧解脫，二、心解脫。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有二種解脫：一、慧解脫，依智慧令心解脫煩惱的繫縛，名慧解脫；二、心解脫，依心清淨解脫煩惱的繫縛，名心解脫。這二種解脫，又由凡聖、淺深差別可分世間及出世間二種，其解脫果及解脫住也有二種差別。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、世間所攝慧解脫、心解脫及二種解脫所得果：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1. 世間慧解脫，指由法住智所攝世間正見的有漏慧，使行者調伏欲的煩惱及色聲香味觸相的繫縛，乃至非想非非想處定以下的煩惱現行；是以世間善惡行、及生起善惡行的因緣為「所行」；以法住智如實知道善惡因果為「體性」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2. 世間心解脫，由世間慧了知心王是染淨依，面對色等境界，能如理作意不與煩惱相應。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3. 世間慧、心二種解脫所得果，能令行者不與煩惱現行相應，出離欲界雜染乃至非想非非想處定以下的煩惱現行而持戒清淨、證得色、無色定等世間靜慮。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、出世間所攝慧解脫、心解脫及二種解脫所得果：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1. 出世間慧解脫，指由無漏慧證法性，證得聖道果，成就涅槃智，令心解脫煩惱縛及相縛。此出世間慧解脫親證法性，當知即是由世間慧及心解脫增上力故，如實了知一切境界；以無分別智為「體性」，由此能如實親證諸法；以真如為「所行」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2. 出世間心解脫，由清淨心增上力故，令五根於五塵境不生雜染，及令六根清淨；最高能入滅盡定。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3. 出世間慧、心二種解脫所得果，能令行者解脫三界一切煩惱縛及相縛。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依體性、因緣、出世間正見所得果區分：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、體性：若世間慧、若出世慧，總略為一，說名正見。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、因緣：正見因緣，當知即是有佛出世、聽聞正法、無倒思惟。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、出世間正見所得果：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1. 辨果相：出世間正見果相即涅槃，是無所對；其能證智是有所對。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2. 辨清淨：由清淨心增上力故，五根於色等所行境界不生雜染，及由意識令諸根順清淨故。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3. 辨依住：入滅盡定時，依壽、煖展轉相依相屬而住。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依世間、出世間二種解脫所得果差別：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、第一義：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1. 世間二種解脫所得果能生後有、不能斷除癡愛種子、無法出離三界。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2. 出世間二種解脫所得果不生後有、能斷除癡愛種子、能出離三界。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、 第二義：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1. 世間二種解脫所得果不與煩惱相應，於所緣境界善惡心互相間雜而生。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2. 出世間二種解脫所得果不被任何境緣染污。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依世間、出世間二種解脫住差別：世間解脫住最高成就非想非非想處解脫，出世間最高成就滅盡定解脫，唯滅盡定具六種寂靜：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、由清淨識沒（前六轉識不現行）平等故，非由彼所依（不是由六根斷滅）平等故。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、於入定時，不由加行，入寂靜故。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、於出定時，不由加行，出寂靜故，次第出故。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、於在定時，三行不行得寂靜故。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、於遠離出心寂靜故，謂於三時。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1. 於阿練若，與同梵行共相雜住時，心恆寂靜。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2. 於聚落中，與諸在家共相雜住時，心恆寂靜。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3. 於二處，與同梵行及在家共相雜住時，心恆寂靜。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、於親近出心寂靜故，謂於三時。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1. 於有色世間勝定出；由次第定入出；屬有相定，由有相作意，入、住、出定。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2. 於無色世間勝定出；由次第定入出；屬有相定，由有相作意，入、住、出定。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3. 於出世間有心定出；不由次第定入出；屬無相定，由無相作意入定、住定；由有相作意出定。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬二、隨別釋2　癸一、世間攝3　子一、慧解脫2　丑一、所行</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨別釋，接著各別解釋，分二科；第一科世間攝，說明屬於世間所攝的慧及心解脫，又分三科；第一科慧解脫，先說明慧解脫，又分二科；第一科所行，說明世間慧所行及因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中依慧解脫，謂世間慧之所行者，當知即是建立惡行及與善行并彼因緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在這二種解脫當中依止慧解脫，約世間慧所活動的境界而言，應當知道就是建立惡行、善行，以及生起惡行及善行的因緣。了知由貪、恚、癡等煩惱心所為因緣，能生身、語、意三種惡行；由無貪、無恚、無癡等善心所為因緣，能生身、語、意三種善行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這段文可對照《中阿含經》211經/大拘絺羅經所說：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　尊者舍黎子問曰： 「賢者拘絺羅！不善者說不善，不善根者說不善根，何者不善？何者不善根耶？」</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　尊者大拘絺羅答曰：「身惡行，口、意惡行，是不善也，貪、恚、癡，是不善根也，是謂不善，是謂不善根。」</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　尊者舍黎子聞已，歎曰： 「善哉！善哉！賢者拘絺羅！」尊者舍黎子歎已，歡喜奉行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　復問曰：「賢者拘絺羅！善者說善，善根者說善根，何者為善？何者（為）善根耶？」</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　尊者大拘絺羅答曰：「身妙行，口、意妙行，是善也，不貪、不恚、不癡，是善根也，是謂為善，是謂善根。」</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、體性</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科體性，說明世間慧解脫的體性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼體性者，當知即是惡行、善行并彼因緣，善不善等體性差別如實正智。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　彼世間慧的體性，應當知道就是對於惡行、善行，及生起惡行、善行的因緣，知道由貪、恚、癡等煩惱心所為因緣，能生身、語、意三種惡行；由無貪、無恚、無癡等善心所為因緣，能生身、語、意三種善行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　要略而言，能如實知道善惡因果的世間正見，是世間慧解脫的體性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》建立惡行等者：墮惡趣業，是名惡行，彼以煩惱為其因緣。生善趣業，是名善行，彼以善法為其因緣。此所建立，名慧所行，世俗諦攝，故是世間。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　造作來生墮到三惡道的身語意業，如殺盜淫妄等十惡業，稱為惡行；惡行是以貪、恚、癡等煩惱為其因緣。造作來生到人天善趣的身語意業，如五戒、十善等，名為善行；善行是以無貪、無恚、無癡等善法為其因緣。建立這些惡行、善行，以及生起惡行、善行的因緣，稱為慧所行。世間慧所緣的善惡行及其因緣，有相、有分別，不離名言相的境界，屬於世俗諦所攝，所以稱為世間。這是先說明世間的慧解脫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p4999"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、心解脫</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科心解脫，說明世間心解脫的體性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又依心解脫，謂心染淨之所依者，當知即是色等境界能取了別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又依心解脫，指生起染污煩惱及清淨善法的依止就是心王，應當知道色聲香味觸法等六塵是心王所取、所了別的境界，能取、能了別色等六塵的是心王，當心王解脫染汙煩惱心所的繫縛，唯與清淨善心所相應，名為心解脫。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這段文可對照《中阿含經》211經/大拘絺羅經所說：（舍利弗）復問曰：「賢者拘絺羅！識者說識，何者識耶？」，尊者大拘絺羅答曰：「識，識（能認識）是故說識。識何等耶？識色，識聲、香、味、觸、法，識識是故說識。」，意指識（六識心王）能認識了別六塵故名識，也就是此處所說：心染淨之所依者，當知即是色等境界能取了別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂心染淨之所依者者：心謂心王，染淨謂彼心所有法。是故說心為彼染淨所依。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　心是心王，指有情的眼識、耳識、鼻識、舌識、身識、意識、末那識、阿賴耶識。染是指心所法的貪、瞋、癡、慢、疑等煩惱心所，淨是指善法的無貪、無瞋、無癡等善心所。因此說心是染法及淨法所依止的處所，心若解脫，就不會被染法所依止，不與染法相應而與善法相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、彼二果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科彼二果，說明世間慧解脫及心解脫的結果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼世間慧心解脫果，當知即是於彼相應、相雜下類雜染出故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依世間慧、心二種解脫所得的果，應當知道就是由世間慧了知善惡行及生起善惡行的因緣，努力修行斷除染法，使後起的心王不與煩惱相應、不再緣所緣相與煩惱和雜而被繫縛，能從欲界下劣種類的煩惱縛中出離。具世間慧的行者若出離欲界的煩惱縛能持戒清淨、或證得禪定（包括未到地定乃最高能得四空定），名世間慧所得心解脫果。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷17窺基大師解釋：「乃至即慧解脫增上力故明心解脫果，謂由前世間慧力故，其心於相應縛及緣縛中出。謂相應者，相應縛也，相雜者，緣縛也。又相應者，俱時起惑，相雜，前後雜生。此是世間心解脫果。唯能不染相應及間生，非離緣縛等，若離者即是無漏心解脫果也。」，意指世間慧心解脫果，能令行者出離相應縛，使心不與煩惱現行俱時相應（如一類得靜慮者可以做到），或令行者暫時不被所緣相繫縛而生煩惱，染淨心前後間雜而生（如未得靜慮，努力受持淨戒者的相貌）。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於彼相應相雜下類雜染出者：欲界煩惱及彼所緣，名下類雜染，由彼欲界最下劣故。彼諸煩惱相應於心，是名相應。彼所緣境與彼煩惱和雜而生，是名相雜。離彼纏縛，是名為出。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲界的煩惱如欲恚害等，以及所緣的色聲香味觸，名下類雜染。因為欲界在三界中是最下品、最低劣的緣故，所以稱為下類雜染。欲界的煩惱與心相應，是名相應。欲界有情的心於緣慮色聲香味觸境時與欲恚害等煩惱和合相雜而生，是名相雜。遠離欲界的煩惱及欲界色聲香味觸境的纏繞與繫縛，名為出。這就是世間的慧解脫及心解脫清淨的相貌。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、出世間攝2　子一、略辨2　丑一、慧所行</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科出世間攝，說明出世間的慧解脫及心解脫，分二科；第一科略辨，要略辨明，又分二科；第一科慧所行，說明出世間的慧所行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">即慧解脫增上力故，出世間慧之所行者，當知即是由世間慧及心解脫增上力故，如實了知一切境界。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依止世間慧解脫的增上力，生起出世間的智慧。出世間智慧所行的真理（約聲聞說是指我空真如），應當知道是由世間慧及世間心解脫的增上力故，也就是由世間慧深信善惡因果所生正見，以及心解脫欲界煩惱及所緣五欲的增上力，依止禪定修四聖諦，證得出世間的無漏智慧，由此能夠如實了知一切境界的真如性。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處論文可對照《中阿含經》211經/大拘絺羅經所說：「賢者拘絺羅！智慧者說智慧，何者智慧？」，尊者大拘絺羅答曰：「知如是故說智慧，知何等耶？知此苦如真，知此苦習、知此苦滅、知此苦滅道如真，知如是，故說智慧。」</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、解脫果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科解脫果，說明出世慧心解脫果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p5000"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">即出世慧心解脫果，當知即是一切種類雜染出故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　即此出世慧心解脫果，能如實了知一切境界的真如性，應當知道這時行者的心能從三界一切種類的煩惱縛與所緣相縛中出離。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前文所說世間慧的心解脫果，只能伏欲界的煩惱縛與所緣相縛；出世間慧的心解脫果能斷除三界一切種類煩惱種子，證入涅槃、出離三界。這是從斷煩惱障來說明心解脫，並不是以斷除定障來說明心解脫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》一切種類雜染出故者：三界煩惱及彼所緣，是名一切種類雜染。永斷彼種，名之為出。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲界、色界、無色界三界的煩惱縛與所緣相縛，是名一切種類雜染。永遠斷除煩惱縛與所緣相縛的種子，說名為出。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、廣釋3　丑一、出體性</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣釋，廣泛詳細解釋出世間慧心解脫果，分三科；第一科出體性，說明出世間慧心解脫果的體性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中若世間慧、若出世慧，總略為一，說名正見。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於此二種解脫慧中世間慧、及出世間的智慧，可以總相要略歸納為一種，稱為正見。世間慧所得正見，是法住智所攝，能厭離欲界欲，出離欲界煩惱證得靜慮；出世慧所得正見，是涅槃智所攝，能厭離三界欲，出離三界煩惱證得涅槃。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這段文可以對照《中阿含經》211經/大拘絺羅經所說：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　復問曰：「賢者拘絺羅！智慧有何義？有何勝？有何功德？」，尊者大拘絺羅答曰：「智慧者有厭義、無欲義、見如真義。」，尊者舍黎子聞已，歎曰：「善哉！善哉！賢者拘絺羅！」。復問曰：「賢者拘絺羅！云何正見？」，尊者大拘絺羅答曰：「知苦如真，知苦習、滅、道如真者，是謂正見。」。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、釋因緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋因緣，解釋得到出世慧正見的因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">正見因緣，當知即是有佛出世、聽聞正法、無倒思惟。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　得到世間、出世間正見的因緣，應當知道就是有佛出世、聽聞正法、無倒思惟。如果佛沒有出現在世間，眾生一輩子乃至生生世世都不知道善惡因果，不知道苦集滅道四諦，也不知道如何修行，所以一定要有佛出世宣說正法，由聽聞正法，並且沒有顛倒錯誤的思惟佛法，才能獲得正見。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這段文可以對照《中阿含經》211經/大拘絺羅經所說：復問曰：「賢者拘絺羅！幾因幾緣生正見耶？」，尊者大拘絺羅答曰：「二因二緣而生正見，云何為二？一者從他聞，二者內自思惟，是謂：二因二緣而生正見。」。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑三、顯得果3　寅一、辨果相2　卯一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科顯得果，顯示出世間正見所得果，分三科；第一科辨果相，說明得到出世間正見的果相，又分二科；第一科標，標出出世間正見所得果相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又出世間正見果相，當知即是前後常故，無所對故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又出世間正見所得的果相，應當知道就是證得不生不滅的涅槃，寂滅涅槃是無為法，沒有前後差別，前後剎那都是常住不變、沒有煩惱流漏、沒有生滅性，是超越有為不可思議的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這段文可以對照《中阿含經》211經/大拘絺羅經所說：（舍利弗）復問曰：「賢者拘絺羅！滅者有何對？」，尊者大拘絺羅答曰：「滅者無有對。」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷17說：「當知即是前後常故，無所對故，是說明我法二空所顯真如，即是正見所了之果。凡夫名前，聖人名後，雖經前後體常不變；不同所學聖道觀待有所餘煩惱故生。」。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又出世間正見果相等者：自內所證無戲論相，名出世間正見果相。依彼正見而得證故，當知即是涅槃離繫果相。由是說彼前後是常，及無所對。如下自釋：若法，所治若有若無、若生不生，常時是有，彼法名無所對。其義應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者由自己內心所證無戲論相，根、塵、識、能所、言語、及器世間都不現，離名言戲論相，名出世間正見果相。依彼出世間正見而得證故，應當知道就是涅槃，涅槃遠離三界煩惱繫縛，是出世間正見的果相。由於涅槃是無為法，是諸法的圓成實性，沒有前後差別，凡位時自性圓成實，或名本來清淨涅槃，入聖位時名清淨圓成實，聲聞聖者名有餘依涅槃、無餘依涅槃，菩薩名無住處涅槃，無論凡、聖體性都是清淨，不需對治，只是凡智不知，聖者已經通達，因此說彼前後是常，及無所對。如下文自會解釋：此出世間正見的涅槃果「法」，「所」對「治」的煩惱不論若有或若無、出世間正見「若生」或是「不生」，正見果無我相無法相，即我法二空真如，或說為涅槃，是常時有的，此正見果是無為法、無所變異、不需對治、沒有生滅，名為無所對。其中的義理應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p5001"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋2　辰一、簡有所對</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科簡有所對，簡別有所對的果相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若法，所治若有，生已無滅；所治若無，滅已有生，彼法名有所對。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若能對治煩惱的正見之「法」，「所」對「治」的煩惱種子若還「有」，仍未斷除的話，於無間道，由出世間正見（正智）「生已」能對治煩惱種子，將煩惱種子對治之後相續「無滅」，這是有學出世間的正見相續。若無學聖者，「所」要對「治」的煩惱種子已斷除滅「無」，前有學金剛喻定無間道能對治的出世間正見（正智）剎那「滅已」，到了解脫道出世間正見相續「有生」（存在）。這有學及無學的出世間正見，是出世間正智（根本智）及世間出世間正智（後得智）所攝，是無漏有為法，剎那生滅相續，名「有所對」。其所證的涅槃是無為法，名「無所對」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷17說：聖道觀待有所餘煩惱故生。所除煩惱若無，不需對治，聖道即滅不起。聖道觀待所治煩惱或有生有滅，故名有對，依此句安立宗旨。下釋有二，先及後順。言若法所治若有，生已無滅者，謂學道法故言：若法，由有所治，若無漏學道相續無滅言：所治若無，滅已有生者，或種斷惡（應當是指所斷惡種）名所治（滅），若學道隨漏（煩惱）故，所治（煩惱）滅已，無學道起故言有生。彼法名有所對者，結彼道諦名為有對。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》的大意是：「若法」指有學聖道法，由於還有所要對治的煩惱，名「所治若有」，若有煩惱生起必須以聖道對治，聖道「生」起對治煩惱「已」後，證入無學法，無學聖道成就，其無漏聖道相續「無滅」。所對治的煩惱若已被對治滅除，名「所治若無」，前有學無漏聖道「滅已」，無學聖道生起，因此說為「有生」。這有學、無學的無漏道諦，隨所對治的煩惱有無而有生有滅，相續不斷，是有為法所攝，名有所對。總說無漏道諦名為「有對」。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》若法所治若有等者：此中法言，意顯正見，無漏有為法所攝故。此為能治，煩惱為其所治。煩惱種子未無餘斷，名所治有。即彼正見生已相續，能為對治，是名生已無滅。若煩惱種已無餘斷，名所治無。然彼正見性有為故，相續滅生，是名滅已有生。如是正見，由生相故說之為有，而非常時，是故名有所對。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處文中所說的法，其意是顯示出世正見，屬於無漏有為法所攝。此出世正見是能對治的聖道，煩惱是所對治法。所對治的煩惱種子若還沒有完全斷除，名「所治有」。若還有煩惱，無漏正見必須生起並且相續不斷，依此能夠對治煩惱，是名「生已無滅」。這是有學出世間的正見相續。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果所對治的煩惱種子已經沒有了，已無餘永斷，稱為「所治無」。雖然煩惱已經對治，前有學正見的體性是有為法，相續滅已，無學正見相續生起，是名「滅已有生」。這有學、無學的無漏正見，在有學位由對治煩惱故而有生相，因此說之為有，在無學位煩惱已斷不需生起對治，其無漏正見仍相續不斷，學、無學的無漏正見是有為法，有生滅相，不像涅槃常時不變，因此名為「有所對」。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、顯無所對</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯無所對，顯示無所對的果相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若法，所治若有若無、若生不生，常時是有，彼法名無所對。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　「若」約無漏正見所證的果「法」而言，「所」對「治」的煩惱不論若有或若無、出世間的無漏正見「若生」或是「不生」，此無漏正見的果「法」無我相無法相，即我法二空真如，或說為涅槃，是常時有的，是無為法、無所變異，名為「無所對」。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》若法所治若有若無等者：此中法言，謂正見果，無漏無為法所攝故。此勝義有，故是常時。所治煩惱若有若無、若生不生，染淨位中無變異故，由是彼法名無所對。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處文中所說的法，是指出世間正見所證的果法，是無漏無為法所攝。此正見果即我法二空真如，屬勝義有，是聖人出世間正智所證的無為理，因此是常時有。無論行者所對治的煩惱若有若無，能對治的出世間正見若生不生，這出世間正見所證的涅槃果法，於染、淨位中都沒有變化差異，在凡夫位名自性清淨涅槃，在有學聖者位名分證涅槃，在無學位名有餘依涅槃，無學壽盡時即入無餘依涅槃，因此涅槃名為無所對。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、辨清淨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨清淨，辨明所得果的清淨相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p5002"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又即此果，由心解脫增上力故，於自所行及彼所依得清淨者，當知即是由清淨心增上力故，於諸色根所行境界不生雜染，及令諸根順清淨故。</span></strong></span></span></p>
