<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又即此出世間正見的果法，由心解脫煩惱縛及相縛的增上力故，於自己五根取色等五境及諸根所依的意根清淨的聖者，應當知道這是由清淨心的強大增上力故，使眼乃至身等色根於所行的色乃至觸等五塵境界不生煩惱等雜染，及令眼乃至意等諸根隨順清淨的緣故。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這段文可以對照《中阿含經》211經/大拘絺羅經所說：尊者舍黎子復問曰：「賢者拘絺羅！有五根異行、異境界，各各受自境界，眼根，耳、鼻、舌、身根，此五根異行、異境界，各各受自境界，誰為彼盡受境界？誰為彼依耶？」，尊者大拘絺羅答曰：「五根異行、異境界，各各自受境界，眼根，耳、鼻、舌、身根，此五根異行、異境界，各各受自境界，意為彼盡受境界，意為彼依。」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這段文在印順法師《佛法概論》中解釋：「意根與五根的關係，可從取境的作用而知。如眼根，像一架照相機，能攝取外境作資料，現為心相而生起眼識。意根是根，所以也能攝取境界。《中含‧大拘絺羅經》說：「五根異行異境界，各各受（取）自境界，意為彼盡受境界」。意根不但有他獨特的（「別法處」）境界，還能承受五根所取的境界。五根如新聞的採訪員，意根是編輯部的外稿搜集者。意根能取五根的所取，又為五根起用的所依。五根與意根的交感相通，即說明了意根為身心和合的中樞。」。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、辨依住</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科辨依住，辨明所得果的依住相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又解脫心住者，當知即是壽之與煖展轉相依相屬而住。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又於出世間慧所得解脫心安住者，此處按下文所說意指欲界或色界行者若安住於想受滅解脫，入滅盡定時，前六轉識及人我見相應的第七識暫不現行，此時如何維持壽命？應當知道就是壽（命根）與煖展轉互相依止、互相繫屬而得安住。這是因為二乘未安立阿賴耶識，入滅盡定時，前六轉識及人我見相應的第七識暫不現行，唯依壽（命根）與煖展轉互相依止互相繫屬而得安住。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼此處說欲界或色界行者若安住於想受滅解脫，壽之與煖展轉相依相屬而住？因為據《阿毘達磨大毘婆沙論》卷153說：問：何故生欲、色界能起滅定，非無色界耶？答：命根依二法轉，一色，二心。此定無心，斷心起故。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、生欲、色界，起此定時心雖斷，而命根依色轉。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、生無色界色雖斷，而命根依心轉。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若生彼起此定者色心俱無，命根無依故應斷，是應名死，非謂入定。是故生彼界不起。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這段文也可對照《中阿含經》211經/大拘絺羅經所說：「&hellip;意者依何住耶？」「意者依壽，依壽住。」「&hellip;壽者依何住耶？」「壽者依暖，依暖住。」「&hellip;壽及暖，此二法為合為別？此二法可得別施設耶？」「壽及暖，此二法合不別，此二法不可別施設。所以者何？因壽故有暖，因暖故有壽。若無壽者則無暖，無暖者則無壽。猶如因油因炷，故得燃燈，彼中因焰故有光，因光故有焰。若無焰者則無光，無光者則無焰。如是因壽故有暖，因暖故有壽。若無壽者則無暖，無暖者則無壽。是故此二法合不別，此二法不可別施設。」。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辛二、彼果差別2　壬一、第一義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科彼果差別，說明世間及出世間二種解脫果的差別，分二科；第一科第一義，依第一種道理說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又此世間及出世間二種解脫果差別者，當知即是於諸受中及因緣中，有癡愛者後有當生，無癡愛者後有不生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又此世間慧所得的心解脫果，及出世間慧所得的心解脫果，這二種解脫果的差別，應當知道就是於世間苦受、樂受、不苦不樂受，或苦樂憂喜捨諸受中，以及生起諸受的因緣中：觸是受因緣，六入是觸因緣，如此展轉上推無明緣行為生起諸受的根本因緣，若唯得世間慧所得的心解脫果的行者，無明愚癡及貪愛的煩惱種子尚未斷除，煩惱種子還會現行，煩惱若現行就會造業，由業感果，下一生還會招感三界苦果；反之若是出世間慧所得的心解脫果者，於觸緣受時，無明愚癡及貪愛的煩惱種子已斷，不再起惑造業，永出三界，來生不會再招感三界苦果。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這段文可對照《中阿含經》211經/大拘絺羅經所說：尊者舍黎子復問曰：「賢者拘絺羅！云何生當來有？」，尊者大拘絺羅答曰：「愚癡凡夫無知、不多聞，無明所覆，愛結所繫，不見善知識，不知聖法，不御聖法，是謂：生當來有。」&hellip; 尊者舍黎子復問曰：「賢者拘絺羅！云何不生當來有？」，尊者大拘絺羅答曰：「若無明已盡，明已生者，必盡苦也，是謂：不生於當來有。」。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於諸受中及因緣中等者：此中因緣，謂即苦觸、樂觸、不苦不樂觸。觸緣受故，名彼因緣。若無明觸所生受及受緣愛，是名有癡愛者。與此相違，名無癡愛。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此苦等諸受中的因緣，就是苦觸、樂觸、不苦不樂觸。因為以觸為緣而有受的緣故，所以說觸為彼諸受的因緣。若接觸境界，不知境界如幻如化，有無明時，由無明觸所生受及受緣愛，由受生起愛煩惱，是名有癡愛者。與此相反，有明相應觸，於明觸所生受不生愛煩惱，名為無癡愛。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬二、第二義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科第二義，依第二種道理說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又彼相雜而相應故，</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又世間慧及心解脫果（世間靜慮），由於無明愚癡及貪愛的煩惱種子尚未斷除，有無明觸所生受，其心與諸煩惱縛及相縛，相雜相應而不能解脫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又彼相雜而相應故者：此顯世間解脫果。由於諸受及因緣中有癡愛故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡是顯示世間慧的解脫果，由世間慧所得的心解脫果於諸受及因緣中有癡愛故，所以稱為相雜。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p5003"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼能依止心法清淨，當知即是非現在緣之所染汙領受彼故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若行者能依止心王的心所法是清淨的，即成就出世間慧所得的心解脫果者，已經斷除煩惱種子，能依心所已得清淨，因此彼清淨心不為現在的所緣境相所染汙，能領受明相應觸所生受，於所緣境不生癡愛。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》彼能依止心法清淨等者：此顯出世間解脫果。由於諸受及因緣中無癡愛故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是顯示出世間慧及心解脫果。由出世間慧所得的解脫果於諸受及因緣中，都是明相應觸所生受，已無癡愛的緣故。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辛三、二解脫住差別2　壬一、列釋6　癸一、識沒寂靜2　子一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科二解脫住差別，說明慧、心解脫二種解脫住的差別，分二科；第一科列釋，列舉出來解釋，又分六科；第一科識沒寂靜，說明識沒寂靜的相狀，又分二科；第一科標，標出差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">即二解脫住差別者，</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又此世間慧心所得的解脫果及出世間慧心所得的解脫住差別方面，即世間慧心所得的解脫果入無想定住（非想非想處定）、出世間慧心所得解脫果入滅盡定住的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這段文可對照《中阿含經》211經/大拘絺羅經所說：尊者舍黎子復問曰：「賢者拘絺羅！若入滅盡定及入無想定者，有何差別？」，尊者大拘絺羅答曰：「比丘入滅盡定者，想及知（受）滅，比丘入無想定者，想、知（受）不滅，若入滅盡定及入無想定者，是謂差別。」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　據印順法師《空之探究》中說：非想非非想處，『中阿含經』作「無想」、「無想處」。無相心定，『中阿含經』每譯作「無想定」。此處經中所說無想定，應指非想非非想處定，這是世間最高的禪定，意識還在，所以說想、知不滅。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》即二解脫住差別者：慧、心解脫，名二解脫。此中義顯，依二解脫入滅盡定所有差別，名二解脫住差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　慧解脫及心解脫這二種，稱為二解脫。這其中的義理顯示，依慧、心解脫二種解脫入滅盡定所有的差別，名為二種解脫住差別。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這段文若對照原文應當是延續前文說明世間及出世間慧、心解脫二種解脫，依此世間二種解脫入無想定（非想非非想處）解脫住及出世間慧分別入滅盡定住的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知即是六寂靜故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　世間慧、心解脫入非想非想處解脫住與出世間慧、心解脫入滅盡定的主要差別，應當了知就是六寂靜，也就是入滅盡定者才有這六種寂靜。如下文說：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、入滅盡定前六轉識心心所法平等不現行，並不是由彼所依六根平等不現行；而凡夫入非想非非想處定，意識還在。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、於入定時，不由加行入寂靜故。〈本地分‧三摩呬多地〉卷12說：「入滅定時，無有分別，我當入定，我當出定。」。入非想非想處定則必須修七作意，如〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷33說：「為離欲界欲，勤修觀行諸瑜伽師，由七作意方能獲得離欲界欲。」&hellip; 如是乃至「為欲證入非想非非想處定，於地地中，隨其所應，當知皆有七種作意。」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又如《大毘婆沙論》卷105說：「於非想非非想處說無相聲者，如說：我多起加行，多用功力，得無相心定，不應於中欣樂染著。」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、出寂靜，出定不由加行，名出寂靜。〈本地分‧三摩呬多地〉卷12說：「將出（滅盡）定時，心先滅故，亦無作意。」，如經中說：「賢者拘絺羅！若從滅盡定起及從無想定起者，有何差別？」，尊者大拘絺羅答曰：「比丘從滅盡定起時，不如是念：『我從滅盡定起。』比丘從無想定起時，作如是念：『我為有想？我為無想？』從滅盡定起及從無想定起者，是謂差別。」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、在滅定三行（身語意）不行，名為寂靜。在非想非非想處定身語不行，意識無明了想相，亦無無想相，但有昧鈍不明了想微細現行，如疑而轉。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、滅定於遠離出心寂靜，滅定名遠離出心恒寂靜。如下文說遠離出三時寂靜。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、滅定於親近出心寂靜，從滅定出入彼三心（色界心、無色定非想非非想處心、無漏心），彼三心親近滅定故，名為親近，此時心寂靜。聖者從出滅盡定能展轉或直入有色定、無色定、或無漏的有心定，於這三種親近出，心恆寂靜。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這段文若依《瑜伽論記》卷17有二種說法：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、六寂靜是：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1. 心遠離沈掉寂靜。依瑜伽論記，清淨識沒平等故者，沒者是沈於定，不沈不沒是平等；並不是由識所依根說平等，因為依根掉動心多浮動，現在因為六識等諸心心所滅不現行，由識不現行而說離彼掉，名依平等。由心遠離沈掉是第一種寂靜。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2. 入寂靜，入定不由加行，名入寂靜。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3. 出寂靜，出定不由加行，名出寂靜。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　4. 在滅定三行不行，名為寂靜。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　5. 於遠離出心寂靜，滅定名遠離出心恒寂靜。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　6. 於親近出心寂靜，從滅定出入彼三心，彼三心親近滅定故，名為親近，此時心寂靜。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、窺基大師說六寂靜：是指下文遠離出心的三時寂靜；於親近出的三心寂靜。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《披尋記》解釋六寂靜是指六識寂靜，依下文所說六寂靜是指由清淨識沒平等故乃至親近出心六種寂靜。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋識沒寂靜。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由清淨識沒平等故，非由彼所依平等故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　入滅盡定時，由於清淨的前六轉識心心所法平等不現行了，並不是由彼所依六根平等不現行，身體還在，只是六識不起現行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這段文可對照《中阿含經》211經/大拘絺羅經所說：尊者舍黎子復問曰：「賢者拘絺羅！若入滅盡定及入無想定者，有何差別？」，尊者大拘絺羅答曰：「比丘入滅盡定者，想及知（受）滅，比丘入無想定者，想、知（受）不滅，若入滅盡定及入無想定者，是謂差別。」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　經說入滅盡定者，想及知滅；入無想定，者想知（受）不滅。意指入非想非想處者，心中非有想，名無想，但不是真實無想，名非無想，這時意識還在；又非入滅盡定，所以說想及知（受）不滅。這意識現不現行是世間慧、心解脫入非想非想處解脫住與出世間慧、心解脫入滅盡定最主要的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》六寂靜故等者：住滅盡定差別有六，此為最初，餘如下說，至文當知。諸心心法滅不現行，名六寂靜。六謂六識，非彼六根，為顯此義，故自釋言：由清淨識沒平等故，非由彼所依平等故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　住滅盡定的差別有六種，這是最初一種，其他的如下文所說，讀到下文時可了知。入滅盡定時，前六識的心王及心所法都止息寂滅而不現行，稱為六寂靜。六是指六識，不是六根，為了顯示這種道理，本論中自己解釋：由於清淨識平等止息不起現行，並不是由識所依的根平等不起。總之不是六根不現行，而是六識不現行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p5004"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、入定寂靜</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科入定寂靜，說明入定寂靜。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於入定時，不由加行入寂靜故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　入滅盡定與一般定不一樣，於入定時不必加功用行作意而入，任運能入寂靜的狀態。如〈本地分‧三摩呬多地〉卷12說：「入滅定時，無有分別，我當入定，我當出定。」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這段文可以對照《中阿含經》211經/大拘絺羅經所說：「賢聖！比丘入滅盡定時，作如是念：『我入滅盡定耶？』」&hellip;「比丘入滅盡定時，不作是念：『我入滅盡定。』然本如是修習心，以是故如是趣向。」。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》不由加行入寂靜故者：謂入定時，進趣所緣皆滅盡故，心便寂滅，由是說言不由加行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈本地分‧三摩呬多地〉卷12說：「依非想非非想處相而入定者，謂於此二心（無所有處地以下的有所有想、無所有處地的無所有想、及非非想）深生厭捨，非想非非想處進趣所緣皆滅盡故，心便寂滅。依滅盡相而入定者，亦復如是。」，因此說不由加行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸三、出定寂靜</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科出定寂靜，說明出定寂靜。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於出定時，不由加行出寂靜故，次第出故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於出滅盡定時，不需加行，心裡不用作意，任運能出寂靜的狀態，次第而出定。本論卷12說：「將出（滅盡）定時，心先滅故，亦無作意。」，又說：「先於其心善修治故。若有諸行、諸狀、諸相，能入於定，能出於定，於彼修習、極多修習；由修習故，任運能入，任運能出。」，入滅盡定的行者於此滅盡定的諸行諸狀諸相善於修治，修習極多修習，由修習故，任運能入、任運能出。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》不由加行出寂靜故等者：出滅定時，任運能出，由是說言不由加行。如其次第觸三種觸而出於定，名次第出。三種觸者，一、不動觸，二、無所有觸，三、無相觸。如本地分說應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/12.htm#49881:10468">陵本十二卷二十一頁1061</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者於入滅定以前先想好什麼時候要出定，出滅定時，任運能出，因此說不由加行。〈本地分‧三摩呬多地〉卷12說：由有境、境境、滅境三種境，於出定時，如它的次第，觸三種觸而出於定，名次第出。出滅盡定時有三種觸：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種不動觸，心不為我慢擾動其心，謂此為我而起我慢，或計未來我當有等，乃至廣說，因此說為觸不動觸。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種無所有觸，緣於境境而出定時，無貪所有、無瞋所有、無癡所有，名無所有觸。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種無相觸，緣於滅境而出定時，於一切相不思惟故緣無相界，出定時還可以進入無相心三昧。如〈本地分‧三摩呬多地〉卷12，438頁所說應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸四、在定寂靜</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科在定寂靜，在定時三行寂靜。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於在定時，三行不行得寂靜故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　正在滅盡定當中也是寂靜，由於身行、語行、意三行不起現行，身沒有出入息、心遠離尋伺不說話，第六意識不起現行，不再思惟，因此證得相似於涅槃的寂靜。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這段文可以對照《中阿含經》211經/大拘絺羅經所說：尊者大拘絺羅答曰：「比丘入滅盡定時，先滅身行，次滅口行，後滅意行。」&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　本論說入滅盡定時先滅語行、次滅身行、後滅意行，此經說先滅身行，次滅口行，後滅意行，這二種說法應當如何會通？本論說若於住時，從第二靜慮已上次第定力，彼三種行次第而滅，無入出息，身行不行，名滅身行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《中阿含經》說先滅身行，應指五識相應名身行，入初靜慮，五識不行，名滅身行；入第二靜慮，尋伺不行，名滅語行；第六意識不行，名滅意行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》三行不行得寂靜故者：身語意行，是名三行。在滅定時，無入出息，身行不行；無有尋伺，語行不行；無有受想，意行不行。由是說言三行不行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　身行、語行、和意行稱為三行。入滅盡定時，沒有出入息了，是身行不行。沒有尋伺心所與意識相應，不說話，是語行不行；沒有受、想心所與意識相應，不再作意思惟，是意行不行。因此說三行不行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p5005"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸五、於遠離出寂靜2　子一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科於遠離出寂靜，說明於遠離出寂靜，分二科；第一科標，標三時寂靜。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於遠離出心寂靜故，謂於三時。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有滅盡定的聖者於遠離出心恆寂靜，這是指心於三個時段能遠離出於雜染、保持寂靜，如下說於阿練若與出家同梵行者雜住、於聚落中與在家者雜住、或於二處與出家、在家共相雜住的三時，心還是出於雜染、保持清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出於遠離出心寂靜相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、於阿練若，與同梵行共相雜住；二、於聚落中，與諸在家共相雜住；三、於二處行相現行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、於阿練若與同梵行共相雜住時，心恆寂靜，沒有世間相應「見聞」諸散亂事。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、於聚落中，與諸在家共相雜住，在村子裡或城市聚落當中，與在家居士雜住時，內心寂靜，沒有世間相應「受用」諸散亂事。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、於二處行相現行，在寂靜的阿蘭若處和眾多人的聚落處，與同梵行或諸在家共相雜住時，內心寂靜，沒有世間相應見聞、受用諸散亂事。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於遠離出心寂靜故等者：此中遠離，謂身遠離。本地分說：身遠離者，謂不與在家及出家眾共相雜住，獨一無侶，是名身遠離。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/30.htm#49890:25163">陵本三十卷八頁2507</a>）今說共相雜住，名遠離出。緣彼雜住不定境界，名於二處行相現行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《披尋記》作者說此處文中所遠離，指身遠離。事實上應該是指「心」遠離。〈本地分〉說：身遠離的行者，不與在家及出家眾共相雜住，獨一沒有伴侶，是名身遠離。如〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷30，1003頁所說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡說的共相雜住，是指由於心能保持寂靜而出於所要遠離的煩惱雜染，名為遠離出，應該是指「心」遠離。由於與在家及出家眾共相雜住不是入定的境界，名於二處行相現行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸六、於親近出寂靜2　子一、正辨出時2　丑一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科於親近出寂靜，說明於親近出寂靜，分二科；第一科正辨出時，正式辨明出定時的寂靜，又分二科；第一科標，標出三時。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於親近出心寂靜故，謂於三時。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　從滅盡定出來入於最先觸入的定，名親近出。心一動，都是寂靜，有三種情況。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這段文可以對照《中阿含經》211經/大拘絺羅經所說：尊者舍黎子復問曰：「賢者拘絺羅！比丘從滅盡定起時，觸幾觸？」，尊者大拘絺羅答曰：「比丘從滅盡定起時觸三觸，云何為三？一者不移動觸，二者無所有觸，三者無相觸，比丘從滅盡定起時觸此三觸。」。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出三時寂靜相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、於有色世間勝定出故；二、於無色世間勝定出故；三、於出世間有心定出故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、於有色世間勝定緣於有境而出定時，無有我慢擾動其心，謂此為我而起我慢，或計未來我當有等，說為觸不動觸；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、於無色世間勝定，緣於境境而出定時，無貪所有無瞋所有無癡所有（意指無貪瞋癡），說為觸無所有觸，心恆寂靜；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、於出世間有心定緣於滅境出定時，於一切相不思惟故緣無相界，由出世間有心定出，入於無相，心恆寂靜，總說名為於三時親近出心寂靜。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以下再詳細說明於三時親近出心寂靜的三種情形：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、於有色世間勝定出故，若配合〈本地分‧三摩呬多地〉卷12所說滅盡定觸三觸而出，這是指觸不動觸而言。有色世間勝定，廣說包括初靜慮乃至第四靜慮，若約最勝指第四靜慮。卷12說入滅定或依非想非非想處相或依滅盡相而入，也從此出。緣非非想心、心所法生厭離心而入彼定，此依初修。依滅盡者即任運緣非非想處心、心所法生厭離等。與前相似，說亦如是，此依久習。又或者說初緣有為行厭捨想心，後緣無為行厭捨想心，厭捨義同，所以說亦如是。這也是約初、久二修的差別。約一般初修得滅盡定的聖者而言；若是這類聖者依九次第定入滅盡定，出滅盡定時應先入無色定中後入色界定，如《瑜伽論記》卷17解釋：這是根據展轉初入無色定中後入色界定心。若是於滅盡定久修，於入住出已得自在的聖者，則可以從任一有色世間勝定入出滅盡定，如《瑜伽論記》卷17解釋：諸佛菩薩從滅定出即可自在入色界定中。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、於無色世間勝定出故，這是觸無所有觸。無色世間勝定，包括空無邊處定乃至非想非非想處定。這是聖者，已離無所有處欲，依非想非非想處相而入於滅盡，出定時還入此非想非非想處定，名於無色世間勝定出故。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、於出世間有心定出故，這是觸無相觸。出世間有心定包括空三摩地、無相心三摩地、無願心三摩地，此處指入無相心三摩地。若行者已得九次第定並成就超越定，心已自在者，依所得四靜慮或下三空定修無相觀，證入無漏的無相三昧，由無相三昧（依滅盡相）入滅盡定，從滅盡定出時，第六識一動名為有心，依無相作意，又入此無相三昧，無漏相應，名於出世間有心定出。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷17說：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、心從滅定出入色界定者：這是根據展轉初入無色定中後入色界定心，也可根據諸佛菩薩從滅定出即可入色界定中。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、若出滅定入無色定時先近入非想非非想定，次入無處有所定，遠入識無邊處定或入空無邊處定。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、若出滅定入無漏心，於下三空隨入一處。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　總之從滅定出先起無色定，次起色界定，或出滅定入無漏定。如此三心由出滅定方起，名「於親近出，心寂靜」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　具有滅盡定的聖者從出滅盡定，能展轉或直入有色定、無色定、或無漏的有心定，於這三種親近出，心恆寂靜。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，關於滅盡定出定觸三種觸而出，說法有很多種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、〈本地分‧三摩呬多地〉卷12說：出滅定時觸三種觸？一、不動觸，二、無所有觸，三、無相觸。這是因為出定時，多由有境、境境、滅境三境而出於定。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1. 有境，有是三有，欲有、色有、無色有；或蘊、處、界稱為有，這是緣內身作無我行而出滅定，不為我慢等動搖，觸不動觸。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2. 境境，是指外六塵，色聲香味觸法的境。這是說出滅定，於境不生貪瞋癡等，觸無所有觸。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3. 滅境，無相稱為滅，緣無相的道理即緣滅境而入定的，也就緣無相而出定。緣於滅境而出定時，於一切相不思惟故，緣無相界，觸無相觸。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、《阿毘達磨大毘婆沙論》卷153說到出滅定時三觸差別有四種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1. 尊者世友作如是說：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（1）空無邊處、識無邊處，是不動觸。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（2）無所有處，是無所有觸。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（3）非想非非想處，是無相觸。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是說從滅盡定出來後有可能到空無邊處、有可能到識無邊處，因為空無邊處與識無邊處也可以稱為不動，相對於下地它都是不動的，所以稱為不動觸。如果是無所有觸，是從滅盡定出來直接到無所有處定裏面。無相觸是從滅盡定出來，直接進入非想非非想處定，這稱為無相觸。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2. 有說：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（1）空，是不動觸。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（2）無願：是無所有觸。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（3）無相，是無相觸。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這位大德沒有說是依止什麼禪定，而說觸不動觸就是進入空三昧，觸無所有觸而出定是進入無願三昧，如果是觸無相觸而出滅盡定的是進入無相三昧。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3. 有說無漏、無所有處、緣涅槃者具名三觸，謂：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（1）無漏，故名不動觸。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（2）無所有處攝，故名無所有觸。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（3）緣涅槃，故名無相觸。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是行者依無所有處定修無相心三昧，緣無相（滅盡相） 入滅盡定，出定時入無漏的無所有處定，約其心無貪等煩惱名觸不動觸；約所入定為無所有處定，名觸無所有觸；約所緣無相涅槃，名觸無相觸。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　4. 大德說曰諸苾芻等出滅定時，</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（1）若起非想非非想處心，不起餘不同分心，當言觸無相觸。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（2）若起無所有處不同分心，當言觸無所有觸。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（3）若起識無邊處不同分心，當言觸不動觸。由此理趣餘五有想定應知亦爾，謂空無邊處及四靜慮（也名觸不動觸）。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、《成唯識論了義燈》卷5：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：入滅定時有二加行。一緣滅受想、二緣無相界；於出定時緣於何境？觸於何觸？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：瑜伽第十二云，出滅定時觸三種觸。一不動觸、二無所有觸、三無相觸。謂出定時多由三境而出於定。一由有境、二由境境、三由滅境。由此三境於出定時，如其次第觸三種觸。如樞要說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又說依初學者，緣滅受想入，緣初二境出，同有為故；依久學者，緣無相入，緣第三境出，同無為故。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若自在者，前隨何境（任何一境）入，後隨何境（任何一境）出。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又未自在，出必定心（出入於定心），在前方便依空等持入，今依空等持出，緣於有境，觸不動觸。依觀五蘊內身無我以為空入，（使）令無我見（不）計內為我名為不動，不為我見之所動故。依無願等持入，緣境境出，觸無所有觸。是五根境之境，名為境境。於六塵境無有貪、瞋．癡故，名無所有觸。依無相等持入，緣滅境出，觸無相觸。以是滅性，名為滅境，無其十相名為無相。初二緣事，後一緣理。然三等持通定及散，未自在者唯依定出，若自在者通依定散，或依空入依無相出。此言觸者非觸塵也，觸謂觸對，即觸心所能令根．境順生心所，以觸境時不起我見、不起貪等、不作相狀，如次即是三觸得名。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這一段大意是說初修還沒有得到滅盡定自在的人，依著三三昧為方便能入滅盡定；依空三昧進入滅盡定，出來就是觸不動觸；如果依無願三昧入滅盡定，出來就是觸無所有觸；依無相三昧入滅盡定，出來是觸無相觸。前面二種是緣事，後面一種是緣理（無相是緣理）。這是沒有自在的人，依什麼定進入、就依什麼定出。如果已經修得自在的就不一樣了，可以自在的從未到地定一直到非想非非想處定都可以修三三昧；乃至現在散心、在欲界定的狀況，也可以思惟空、無相、無願的道理，所以它是通於定散的。已經自在的人依定心或散心都可以入出滅盡定，這是程度非常非常高的聖人，就是佛及八地以上的菩薩或者是一分（少分）的廣慧聲聞才可以，一般聖者沒辦法如此。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、《瑜伽論記》卷4所說不出如上所舉三種解釋，其文如下：出定緣三種境，觸三種觸者。若依小乘婆沙正理及成實論等皆廣說之。且引正理第十二卷云，如契經說出滅定時當觸三觸，謂不動觸、無所有觸及無相觸。何者、云何觸此三觸？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1. 有說，滅定起心相應有空無願無相三觸，如其次第出滅定時觸於三觸。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2. 有餘師說，識處、空處心相應觸名不動觸，此二純作識空相故；無所有處心相應觸名無所有觸，無先所有故；非想非非想相應觸名無相觸，想無想相不分明故。即由此故說四無色。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3. 若有想定從滅定起心通有漏無漏。滅定起時或逆次第入諸等至，或逆超越入諸等至，容有起滅定心現在前故。復有餘師說，唯約無漏。有處緣涅槃心起滅定時言觸三觸，以無漏故名為不動，無所有處地所攝故名無所有，緣涅槃故名為無相。解云，如摩訶俱稀羅經作如是說當觸故。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此三師各釋不同。初師說者，謂我我所執掉舉名動，空無我行能對治行故，能破動故名為不動，不動相應觸名不動觸；貪心執境攝為己有，有所執故名所有，無願三摩地能斷所有名無所有，餘如前說；生死十相，涅槃中無為無相，無相即定，緣無相故為無相，餘如前說。此是三觸體性。無心時無此等觸，出時忽遇，名門中行，忽遇壁等，是謂三觸之義。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二說者，謂識處方便唯觀於識，空處方便亦唯觀空，無異想故名為不動，彼相應觸名不動觸。根本地中雖通異相從方便說皆名不動；無所有處無先遍識所有名無所有；有頂地中無有想無想二分明想故名無想，乃至有頂不可言無想故，四無色皆名有想，是謂三觸體。起滅定心通有漏，若有漏者，若逆次入非想等至，名觸無相觸；若逆超入無所有處及無漏，逆次第入無所有想皆觸無所有觸；若無漏逆超入識處，名觸不動觸。雖不定得入空處，以二處皆名不動觸一，即是其名。又釋，此師非薩婆多正宗義，是異師計從滅，空處等故作是釋。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三說者，但取一念無漏無所有處緣滅諦涅槃，以約諦是無漏、非有漏故名不動；約地名為無所有處，約所緣名無相。彼相應觸具三種名，入彼心時名三觸。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　今此文中有二師釋。初此與婆沙正理等異，謂出定時多由三境。一緣有境而出定時無我等動觸者，此緣內身作無我行而出滅定不為我慢等動。二緣道諦，道能取境，今出滅定能緣境，道諦為境名取境，取境不生貪等，觸無所有觸，以道不能增長貪瞋等或名觸無所有觸。相不思惟故緣無相界，是故說言觸無相觸者，若緣滅諦出滅定時，名緣滅境離眾相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二云：此依未自在義要次第故。以定心出觸不動觸是空等持，觸無所有觸是無願等持，觸無相觸是無相等持。依自在者。超一切地隨其所起定、或散、緣理、緣內、緣外，觸三種觸。內三（受想行）有體名有境，外六塵名境境，無相理名滅境。由入滅定折伏心已，煩惱不動，三根不擾非相所亂，唯以善心而出於定。今觀文意多依定心出觸三種觸故也。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p5006"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於親近出心寂靜故者：滅定出時，餘定現前，最鄰近故，名親近出。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由滅盡定出來，其餘定心現前，最鄰近滅盡定，因此名親近出。親近出就是出滅盡定時最先入的定，因此親近出的出，指出滅盡定。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、更顯諸定2　丑一、獲得</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科更顯諸定，進一步顯示出滅盡定後的諸定，分二科；第一科獲得，說明諸定的獲得。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又此諸定非唯滅定出已方得，亦先已得，今起現前。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又前文說的有色世間勝定、無色世間勝定，及出世間無漏的有心定，這三種定並不是出了滅盡定才獲得，而是以前就已經成就這些定，從這些定入滅盡定，現在從滅盡定出來就現前了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷17說：亦先已得今起現前，是根據過去曾得種類，因此說先得。也有未曾得，從滅盡定出才起，因此說「亦」先已得。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又《阿毘達磨大毘婆沙論》卷153：「入滅定心，通曾得未曾得，出滅定心唯曾得。」。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、清淨2　寅一、由次第定</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科清淨，說明清淨的獲得，分二科；第一科由次第定，說明由次第定獲得。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中前二，由次第定故，展轉獲得勝定清淨。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處所說前二種有色世間勝定、無色世間勝定，是由修九次第定故，展轉獲得殊勝定力所得的清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、不由次第定</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不由次第定，說明不由次第定獲得。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">後一，不由次第定故，然由通達無相界故，展轉獲得勝定清淨。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　後一種出世間無漏的有心定，不是由次第定所得，是由通達無相界，依不思惟一切相或正思惟無相，而展轉獲得勝定清淨。依色界四靜慮中任何一靜慮，或無色界四空定中除非想非非想處定外之任何一定，都可以修無相三昧，所以說不由次第定獲得定清淨。這是說明世間定及出世間定的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《成唯識論了義燈》卷5說：依初學者，緣滅受想入，緣初二境出，同有為故；依久學者，緣無相入，緣第三境出，同無為故。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬二、料簡2　癸一、有相定</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科料簡，詳細思惟簡別有相定及無相定的差別，分二科；第一科有相定，說明入有相定的作意。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有相定，由有相作意，入、住、出定。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又所有的有相定，都是由有相作意，才能夠入定、住定、及出定。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前面是略釋，要略舉出來解釋滅盡定六種寂靜的相貌，現在是料簡，從滅盡定出來以後，世間的定也是清淨，因為心中已經完全沒有煩惱的流漏，所以說是清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、無相定</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科無相定，說明入無相定的作意。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若無相定，由無相作意入定、住定；由有相作意，當知出定。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若是無相定，是由無相作意，才能夠入定及住定；於無相定若生起有相作意，應當知道由此有相作意，就出定了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　據《空之探究》說：「定，有有想與無想的二類」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如《雜阿含經》卷21（大正2，146c）說：尊者阿難語迦摩比丘言：若比丘，離欲惡不善法，有覺有觀，離生喜樂，初禪具足住；如是&hellip;&hellip;無所有入處具足住：如是有想比丘有法而不覺知。&hellip;&hellip;</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　比丘一切想不憶念，無想心三昧身作證具足住，是名比丘無想於有法而不覺知。 無所有處以下，是初禪到無所有處定，是有想而不覺知；無想心定是無想而不覺知。《增支部》與此相當的，也說無所有處以下，是有想而不覺知；接著說不踊不沒（即「不低不昂」）的三昧。這可見無所有處以上，就是無想的無相心三昧。&hellip;&hellip;</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　「『中部』的非想非非想處，『中阿含經』作「無想」、「無想處」。無相心定，『中阿含經』每譯作「無想定」。無想（無相心）定與非想非非想處定，無想定，滅盡定，有著複雜的關係。」</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無相，在解脫道中，有種種名稱，如無相心解脫、無相心三昧、無相解脫、無相三昧、無相等至、無相住。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無相定，依修行者的用心不同，淺深不一；與成為定論的非想非非想處，滅盡定，無想定，都有關係，所以內容比較複雜。《大毘婆沙論》卷104說：謂無相聲，說多種義：1.或於空三摩地說無相聲。 2. 如是或於見道，3. 或於不動心解脫 ，3. 或於非想非非想處，5. 或即於無相三摩地說無相聲。（大正27，541b6〜9）</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《大毘婆沙論》認為「無相」這一語詞，含有五種不同的意義：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1. 空三摩地。（參見《大毘婆沙論》卷104，大正27，541b9〜c15）</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2. 見道。（參見《大毘婆沙論》卷105，大正27，541c15～542a1）</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3. 不動心解脫。（參見《大毘婆沙論》卷105，大正27，542a1~6）</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　4. 非想非非想處。（參見《大毘婆沙論》卷105，大正27，542a6~12）</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　5. 無相三摩地。（參見《大毘婆沙論》卷105，大正27，542a12~14）</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《大毘婆沙論》認為：「無相」這一名稱，有五種不同的意義，然從經文來說，也許還不止於所說的五義呢！</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無相心三昧，是有淺深的：淺的還可能會退墮；深的是見滅得道，成為聖者；最究竟的，當然是一切煩惱空，阿羅漢的不動心解脫了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無相心三昧通於有漏、無漏，有各種意義，如下：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、無相心三昧，「是智果智功德」，是無漏的。《瑜伽論記》卷17說：有學聖者於無相定勤修學故，又即於此多修習故，永斷三界修斷我慢。由此斷故，說名無學。智果、智功德的無相心三昧，《大毘婆沙論》認為是空三摩地的別名。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依經文所說，無相心三昧，或在無量心解脫以下說，那是「出離一切相」，心「不為隨相識所纏縛」的。或依四禪說無相心三昧，如不再進求，與眾人往來雜處，戲笑調弄，那是會退墮，可能還俗的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無相心三昧通於有漏、無漏；智果智功德的無相心三昧，也就是無相心解脫，唯是無漏的（初果到四果）。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、無相心三昧，別開為二種無想心定。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在經中，無相心三昧，開為二種無想心定：1. 非想非非想處定，2. 滅盡定。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1. 以非想非非想處說無相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（1） 無相心三昧而被解說為「非想非非想處」的，如《大毘婆沙論》卷105說：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於非想非非想處說無相聲者，如說：我多起加行，多用功力，得無相心定，不應於中欣樂染著。此說不起有頂味定，唯起淨定。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：何故非想非非想處名無相耶？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：彼無明了想相，亦無無想相，但有昧鈍不明了想微細現行，如疑而轉，故名無相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（2） 經說無相定，而被解說為非想非非想處定的，是《中阿含經》的《淨不動道經》。經上說：欲想，色想，不動想，無所有處想，「彼一切想是無常法，是苦，是滅，彼於爾時而得無想。彼如是行，如是學，如是修習而廣布，便於此得心淨。&hellip;&hellip;或於此得入無想，或以慧為解」。得此無想定的，如有所受（取）：樂、著、住，就會受（非）有想無想處的果報。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無相心定被開為非想非非想處定及滅盡定二種無想心定的原因是：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（1） 於無相心定有所樂著，所以是無想而又有不明了的細想現行，因而名為非想非非想處定。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（2） 如心無取著，那就是無相心解脫了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2. 以想受滅定說無相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（1） 想受滅定，或名滅（盡）定，或名增上想滅智定。與無相心三昧相當的，如《相應部》〈目犍連相應〉：從初禪說到四禪，從空無邊處到非想非非想處；在八定以上，說無相心定。而〈舍利弗相應〉，也從初禪說到非想非非想處定，然後說想受滅定。可見無相心三昧、與想受滅定的地位相當。&hellip;&hellip;滅盡定在佛教界是多有諍論的。「想受滅定」是從「無相心定」中分化出來的，當然久已為佛教界所公認，然於非想非非想處以上，立滅盡定的，如《中部》《撒餌經》等，而在《中阿含經》中，僅與《撒餌經》相當的（178）《獵師經》，在非想非非想處以上，立「想知滅」，其餘都沒有，可見部派間所誦的經教，想受滅定還在不確定狀態中。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（2） 滅盡定與無想──無相心定，《中阿含經》辨別二定的入定與出定的差別，而《中部》卻沒有。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　想受滅定，在佛教界是多有諍論的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　‧如烏陀夷反對舍利弗所說的：「若於現法不得究竟智，身壞命終，過摶食天，生餘意生天中，於彼出入想知滅定，必有此處」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　‧在部派中，或說想受滅定是有為的；或說是無為的；或說是非有為非無為的。或說想受滅者是無想有情；或說非無想有情；或說世間想受滅是無想有情，出世想受滅是聖者。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　‧大乘經以為：菩薩如悲願不足而入滅定，是會證小果的；如悲願具足，那就是證入如如法性的深定了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這樣的異說紛紜，足以說明，與無相心定有關的滅盡定，在佛教界是非常暗昧的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3. 以無想有情、無想定說無相依無相心三昧，演化出非想非非想處定（及報處），滅盡定以外，還有無想有情、無想定。無相心三昧不作意一切相，也就是不起一切想。&hellip;&hellip;</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無想定與無想有情，可能外道有類似無想的修驗與傳說，佛法為了要給以應有的解說，才從無相定、滅盡定中分出，位居四禪廣果天上。這是成立要遲一些。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　4. 以見道說無相。如《大毘婆沙論》卷40（大正27，209b）說：見道名為無相住故。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　5. 凡夫的無相心三昧（無想定及非想非非想處定）及聖者的無相心三昧（見道、智果智功德、滅盡定）的差別：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（1）凡夫的無相心三昧：淺的還會退墮。（有漏的無相心三昧）</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（2）聖者的無相心三昧：若是深的見道、智果智功德不會退，若是滅盡定尚未自在者也有退的可能，如《大毘婆沙論》卷153說：以是義故，知滅盡定，欲界初起，退生色界復能現前；餘不能起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p5007"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由次第定等者：本地分說：云何無間入諸等至？謂如有一，得初靜慮乃至有頂，然未圓滿清淨鮮白。先順次入乃至有頂，後逆次入至初靜慮。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/12.htm#49908:9572">陵本十二卷四頁976</a>）其義應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈本地分〉說：如何能夠無間入諸禪定？是指如有一類行者，證得初靜慮乃至三有之頂的非想非非想處定，然而所修的禪定沒有圓滿清淨鮮白。先依順次第，依次入初靜慮、第二靜慮、第三靜慮、第四靜慮、空無邊處定、識無邊處定、無所有處定，乃至非想非非想處定；依逆次第，後又從非想非非想處定退到無所有處定、識無邊處定、空無邊處定、第四靜慮、第三靜慮、第二靜慮到初靜慮，在禪定境界中沒有間隔地順逆次第入定。如〈本地分‧三摩呬多地〉所說，其中的義理應可了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">己三、法因緣經2　庚一、標所釋經</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科法因緣經，引釋《法因緣經》，分二科；第一科標所釋經，標出所釋經名。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，當釋法因緣經。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，應當解釋《法因緣經》的要義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">庚二、廣顯彼義4　辛一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣顯彼義，廣泛顯示《法因緣經》的義理，分四科；第一科標，標出八相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂於阿毗達摩、阿毗毗奈耶中，善巧苾芻、或鄔波索迦，欲依解了而請問者，當依八相而興請問。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　「阿毗達摩」，阿毗，是對向的意思；達摩是法，阿毗達摩名對法，也就是論。「阿毗毗奈耶」，阿毗，是對向；毗奈耶是律或調伏，阿毗毗奈耶是對向律或對向調伏。佛陀在所說的論及律中，開示：若有善巧的苾芻即比丘，鄔波索迦是優婆塞，也就是近事男，想要了解佛說的法義，或如何修行的道理而請法時，應當依止八種相而發起請問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辛二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等八相？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪八種相？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辛三、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科列，列出八相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂解了事、解了所治、解了果、解了自性、解了果差別、解了所依、解了功德、解了證得。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依八相來請法，包括：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、解了事，必須理解明了所知事；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、解了所治，理解明了所對治的煩惱；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、解了果，理解明了對治的結果；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、解了自性，理解明了修道的自性；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、解了果差別，理解明了各種斷滅果的差別相；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、解了所依，理解明了各種斷滅的所依處；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、解了功德，理解明了功德；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八、解了證得，理解明了證得的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辛四、釋8　壬一、解了事</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科釋，解釋八相的內容，分八科；第一科解了事，理解明了所知事的要義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="62p5008"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">解了事者，謂能解了五取蘊故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　理解明了所知事方面，是指能理解明了五取蘊。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有情的五取蘊是由煩惱而生，依五取蘊又能生煩惱的有漏五蘊。有情所有的煩惱、痛苦、造業都是依此而生，五取蘊是生死的根本所依。如《雜阿含經》卷3，尊告諸比丘：「有五受陰？謂色受陰，受、想、行、識受陰。愚癡無聞凡夫無慧無明，於五受陰生我見繫著，使心繫著而生貪欲。比丘！多聞聖弟子有慧有明，於此五受陰不為見我繫著，使心結縛而起貪欲。云何愚癡無聞凡夫無慧無明，於五受陰見我繫著，使心結縛而生貪欲？比丘！愚癡無聞凡夫無慧無明，見色是我、異我、相在。如是受、想、行、識，是我、異我、相在。如是愚癡無聞凡夫無慧無明，於五受陰說我繫著，使心結縛而生貪欲。」</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　經中說明凡夫執五蘊為我我所，而起惑造業輪轉生死，若想出離三界乃至求證無上菩提，都要斷除執五蘊為我我所的執著，才能成就。因此求法者應先了解五取蘊的因緣果相。本論〈決擇‧五識身相應地意地〉卷53到57中蘊善巧，有詳細說明五取蘊的各種差別相，其他經論也多處說到五取蘊，讀者可以多方參究。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬二、解了所治2　癸一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科解了所治，說明理解明了所治的要義，分二科；第一科標，標出二種所治。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">解了所治者，謂愛雜染及見雜染。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二應當理解明了所對治的煩惱方面，包括分別起與俱生起的愛煩惱及見煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　愛煩惱，貪染之心名之為愛，若迷於假、實之事，隨心所對一切事境生起染著纏綿，通名為愛。例如天台宗所說五鈍使之貪、瞋、癡、慢、疑等一切迷事煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　見煩惱，邪心觀理名之為見，若迷於假實之理，而倒想邪求、隨見偏理妄執為實，通名為見。例如五利使之身見、邊見、邪見、見取、戒禁取等。於事理二法顛倒染著的二種妄心，即見煩惱與愛煩惱的合稱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　愛煩惱及見煩惱的自性、差別，於〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷8，及〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷58及卷59，有詳細說明，了解招感生死的愛煩惱及見煩惱，並勤修戒定慧加以對治，才能夠出離生死，到達涅槃的彼岸。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、釋2　子一、愛雜染</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋二種所治，分二科；第一科愛雜染，說明愛雜染的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由愛雜染故，於後有滅不生欣樂。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於有愛的煩惱，就會染著色身，於今生所得五蘊生起自體愛、於來生所得五蘊生起後有愛；染著於境界，於未得所求境界，或為和合，或為不離，或為增益，生起彼彼喜樂愛；於將得現前境界、及於已得未受用境、并於現前正受用境，期望不相離久住，生起喜貪俱行愛；由此不願出離生死、染著生死、不好樂涅槃，對於後有五蘊的寂滅不生歡欣好樂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、見雜染</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科見雜染，說明見雜染的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由見雜染故，雖生欣樂而不能證。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於有見的煩惱，了解愛是不好的，可是思想有錯誤，有邪見，也可能有外道的常見、或斷見，常斷二見都由身見而來，於是由斷見於後有滅雖生欣樂而不能證；雖然想離欲，也想要得定趣向涅槃，因為思想、方法錯誤而不能證得。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬三、解了果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科解了果，說明理解明了果的要義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">解了果者，謂此二種雜染永斷。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　理解明了修道所證的結果方面，是指於此愛煩惱及見煩惱二種雜染永遠斷除，證得圓滿的聖道果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬四、解了自性2　癸一、出道支</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科解了自性，說明了解修道的自性，分二科；第一科出道支，說明以道支為自性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">解了自性者，謂八聖支道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　理解明了修道的自性方面，是指必須深刻的了解修行的方法就是八正道：正見、正思惟、正語、正業、正命、正精進、正定、正念。支是因，道是道路，聖人通達涅槃的道路，名八聖支道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、廣差別3　子一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>
